1935.11.02

Sixth Plenary Session Inauguration Ceremony Completed: President Wang Targeted by Assassin 1

Shot three times; immediately sent to the Central Hospital for treatment. Assailant Sun Fengming and accomplice apprehended on the spot.

Meeting continued as scheduled after the incident.

(Nanjing) This morning, after the conclusion of the Sixth Plenary Session's opening ceremony, at 9:30 AM, while a photograph was being taken at the entrance of the First Conference Hall, two assassins wielding handguns opened fire on Wang Jingwei. Wang was struck three times and collapsed. Central Committee member Zhang Ji seized the assailant Sun Fengming from behind, embracing him around the waist, while Zhang Xueliang knocked the gun from his hand and kicked him to the ground. Wang's guards opened fire, hitting the assailant, who was apprehended on the spot. Chiang Kai-shek was inside at the time. Subsequently, military police secured the entrances to the Party Headquarters and conducted a search, apprehending six suspects, including one woman who also carried a handgun. Based on their actions, the intended target appeared to be more than just Wang.

Military Police Search "Chenguang News Agency"

The assassins were able to infiltrate the venue by recently registering with the Central Party Headquarters under the guise of operating the "Chenguang News Agency" and obtaining access passes. The registered president was named Hu Yunqing. When military police rushed to search the agency, the premises were already deserted. Documents had been burned, and embers were still smoldering. Examination of the remaining fragments of text revealed much inflammatory propaganda.

Wang Is Conscious and Out of Danger

After Wang was taken to the Central Hospital, diagnosis by Liu Ruiheng and Shen Kefei revealed that the bullet wounds were not deep, and no major blood vessels were ruptured. An X-ray was scheduled for the afternoon. Wang's mind was very clear. Liu Ruiheng stated that if there were no post-operative complications, his life should be out of danger.

Foreign Envoys Offer Condolences to President Wang

(Nanjing) After learning that President Wang had been wounded by an assassin, the U.S. Embassy in China sent condolences to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs on the afternoon of the same day, expressing deep concern for Wang's condition. (Central News Agency dispatch, 1st)

(Nanjing) The Japanese Embassy sent Secretary Matsumura on the 1st to represent Ambassador Arita in conveying condolences to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for President Wang. Military Attaché Amemiya also visited the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to offer condolences. In addition, Soviet Ambassador to China Bogomolov visited Tang Youren at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs at around 3:00 PM on the 1st to personally convey his condolences. (Central News Agency dispatch, 1st)

(Nanjing) After news of Wang's assassination attempt spread, German Ambassador Trautmann personally visited the Ministry of Foreign Affairs at 11:50 AM on the 1st to offer condolences. In the afternoon, Secretary Feller of the Italian Embassy also visited the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to represent Italian Ambassador Lojacono in offering condolences. (Central News Agency dispatch, 1st)

(Nanjing) Upon learning that Wang had been wounded by an assassin, the Japanese Embassy in China immediately sent Secretary Matsumura to represent Ambassador Arita in conveying condolences to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. Military Attaché Amemiya also visited the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to offer condolences. In addition, the Russian Ambassador visited Vice Minister Tang at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs in the afternoon to personally convey his condolences. (Special dispatch, 1st)

The Assailant Remains Silent Under Interrogation

When the assailant Sun Fengming was captured, he was also shot in the leg by Wang's guards. He was also injured in the chest by police officers while the gun was being seized. He was also sent to the Central Hospital. Under interrogation by the police, he remained silent, only stating that he was from Xuzhou and had served as a platoon leader in a certain army.

Chiang Kai-shek Personally Watched Over Him at the Hospital for Several Hours

After Wang was shot, Chiang immediately ordered doctors to be summoned by telephone and personally directed the stretcher bearers at the hospital, appearing very anxious. After Wang arrived at the hospital, Chiang rushed there and watched over him for several hours. All the other Central Committee members also went to the hospital to visit him. Wang's wife, Chen Bijun, remained calm after Wang was shot, embracing Wang and comforting him, saying that it was to be expected that a revolutionary leader would be targeted by assassins.

President Wang, Attacked Yesterday

Internal Security Check Conducted at Central Party Headquarters

After the incident, the Central Party Headquarters was sealed off. Everyone inside, except for Central Committee members, including Party officials and news reporters, were subjected to a security check by military police before being allowed to leave at 2:00 PM. It was reported that a few minutes after the gunshots were heard, a man in a Western suit reported the assassination attempt by telephone to the Public Relations Department. Party Headquarters staff suspected him of being an accomplice and turned him over to the police. A stray bullet passed through the trouser leg and sock of Central Committee member Zhou Qigang without causing injury. Zhang Chong, head of the Film Department, confirmed that the assassin's handgun was a revolver, with two bullets remaining unfired. (Special dispatch, 1st)

(Nanjing) The Sixth Plenary Session, which was the focus of national attention, held a solemn and grand opening ceremony at 9:00 AM on the 1st. Unexpectedly, after the ceremony concluded and all the Central Committee members had finished taking a photograph, a serious assassination attempt occurred, resulting in Central Executive Committee member and President of the Executive Yuan, Wang Jingwei, being shot by the assassin Sun Fengming. This was an unprecedented and shocking crime at the Central Party Headquarters, and all parties are paying extraordinary attention to it. The assassin Sun Fengming and two accomplices were all arrested on the spot. The details are as follows:

Assassin Strikes: At 9:00 AM on the 1st, all Central Committee members held the opening ceremony of the Sixth Plenary Session in the Central Auditorium, presided over by Committee Member Wang, who also delivered the opening address. After the ceremony, all Central Committee members went to the entrance of the First Conference Hall to take a photograph. During the photograph, the Central Committee members stood in five rows. Wang, along with Zhang Jingjiang, Yan Xishan, Zhang Xueliang, and other committee members, were in the first row for the photograph, which was completed at 9:35 AM. The committee members then turned to return to the conference hall. Unexpectedly, at this moment, the assassin opened fire on President Wang.

Wang Wounded: The assassin, Sun Fengming, was dressed in a Western suit and wore a jacket. During the photograph, he mingled among the audience near the cameras with two accomplices, showing no unusual behavior, so he did not attract attention. When the photograph was finished and the committee members turned to return to the conference hall, the assassin suddenly emerged from the crowd, pulled a handgun from his jacket pocket, and fired repeatedly at President Wang, catching everyone off guard. President Wang immediately fell to the ground.

Assassin Captured: When the assassin fired the gun, Central Committee member Zhang Ji, who was standing next to President Wang, immediately rushed behind the assassin and embraced him tightly around the waist. However, the assassin continued to fire wildly, for a total of about seven or eight shots. At this time, Zhang Xueliang had also rushed to the front of the assassin and kicked him to the ground. President Wang's guards also raised their guns and fired one shot at him. The assassin immediately fell to the ground, and the two accomplices standing behind the assassin immediately ran away, but were eventually apprehended by the guards.

Sent to the Hospital: When President Wang was wounded and fell to the ground, Committee Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, who had already stepped into the door, ran out upon hearing the gunshots. Seeing the situation, he immediately stepped forward to help President Wang up, and with the assistance of other committee members, carried him to the conference room. He immediately used the telephone to notify the Central Hospital. The hospital director, Liu Ruiheng, and the chief of surgery, Shen Kefei, immediately rushed to the Central Party Headquarters in an ambulance. After bandaging President Wang's wounds slightly, they had him lie on the ambulance bed. Chiang Kai-shek, Kong Xiangxi, Chu Minyi, Chen Shuren, and Wang's wife, Chen Bijun, carried him onto the ambulance and sent him to the Central Hospital for treatment. Chiang Kai-shek and Chen Bijun accompanied him personally. Chiang Kai-shek then returned to the Central Party Headquarters to attend the meeting.

Page 4

Wounds Not Serious: It is reported that President Wang's injuries are not serious. (The Central Hospital's medical record is recorded separately). After the assassin Sun Fengming was shot, he was also transported to the Central Hospital for treatment, hoping to obtain a confession. Apart from President Wang, no other Central leaders were injured. Only one worker was hit by a stray bullet in the leg, but it is not a serious injury.

More Suspects Apprehended: After the incident occurred, the police officers serving as guards at the Central Party Headquarters immediately took action and imposed martial law, cutting off traffic and conducting searches. Police Chief Chen Zhuo and Gendarmerie Commander Gu Zhenglun personally directed the searches, which were completed at around 1:00 PM. Several more suspects were subsequently arrested.

Committee Members Visit: The preparatory meeting of the conference still opened at 10:30 AM, with Chairman Yu Youren expressing his regret. Zhang Ji also gave a detailed account of witnessing the assassin commit the crime and being captured. All the committee members present were deeply saddened by this unfortunate incident and went to the hospital to visit after the meeting.

The Case Is Under Investigation: The assassin, Sun Fengming, is a field reporter for the Nanjing Chenguang News Agency, in his twenties. On the 31st, he obtained access pass number 63 from the Central Party Headquarters press reception desk. No one suspected that he would commit this unlawful act. When the incident occurred, the military police immediately rushed to the agency to surround and search it. All personnel had already fled before the incident occurred. All documents were also burned in the stove. Only a letter left on the desk was found, with the words "Leave for those who come" written on the envelope, and the words "The affairs of this agency have nothing to do with Guo Zhimou, Wu Huang, and Zhou Xiling. We hereby declare" written on the note. The handgun used in the assassination was seized on the spot. It was a Spanish-made six-shot revolver, gun number 8679. According to the assassin, it was purchased in Shanghai. All six bullets had been fired. Five empty shell casings were left in the cylinder. The reporter access pass worn by the assassin was introduced by Guo Zhimou to Wu Huang and Zhou Xiling, so they were able to obtain it from the Central Party Headquarters. According to current investigations, the assassin's intention to assassinate was not initially limited to Wang alone, and the arrangements before and after the event were meticulously planned, making them undoubtedly communist bandits. The remaining members of the group are now being closely pursued in order to bring them to justice and punish them. Of the ten or more suspects apprehended today, some were those who acted hastily and did not heed police instructions during the incident at the Central Party Headquarters, and some were those who followed Chiang Kai-shek to and from the mausoleum this morning, acting suspiciously. The adjutant recorded their vehicle license plate numbers and notified them to be detained after the incident occurred. They are now being interrogated in detail in order to get to the bottom of the matter. (Central News Agency dispatch, 1st)

Party Headquarters Closed: After the unfortunate incident occurred, the Standing Committee immediately decided to temporarily close the Central Party Headquarters during the Sixth Plenary Session and the Fifth National Congress, and the Secretariat issued the following notice: "According to the Standing Committee's discussion, all staff members of the Party Headquarters, except those with duties at the Secretariats of the Sixth Plenary Session and the Fifth National Congress, will be given a holiday after inspection during the sessions. Regular access passes will not be valid. This is hereby announced. Central Secretariat." (Central News Agency dispatch, 1st)

Chiang Kai-shek and Others Did Not Visit the Hospital

(Nanjing) President Wang is staying in room 251 of the Central Hospital. After 11:00 AM, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, Kong Xiangxi, He Yingqin, Yan Xishan, Yang Yongtai, Chen Cheng, Xu Mo, Zhu Peide, and more than 100 Central Committee members in Nanjing went to visit. Only Chiang Kai-shek and Kong Xiangxi personally entered Wang's room. Chiang Kai-shek and Kong Xiangxi personally conveyed their condolences. Wang wanted to talk a little, but Chiang asked him to rest and recuperate, and then took his leave. According to Chu Minyi, who spoke to Central News Agency reporters at the hospital at 1:35 PM, Wang's injuries have been confirmed to be only injuries to the back ribs, and a detailed examination will be performed in the afternoon before surgery. Doctors have examined Wang's body temperature and found it to be 37.8 degrees, with a pulse of 88 beats per minute. Wang's wife, Chen Bijun, and his sons and daughters, as well as Zeng Zhongming, are all at the hospital attending to him. Wang's spirits are excellent and he speaks as usual, frequently saying, "My injuries are not serious, don't panic." (Central News Agency dispatch, 1st)

Good Spirits After Surgery

(Nanjing) After President Wang was unfortunately targeted by the criminal Sun Fengming, all the important figures in the Central government were extremely indignant about this matter. Chiang Kai-shek, Yan Xishan, Zhang Xueliang, Sun Ke, Dai Jitao, Ju Zheng, Yu Youren, and all the Central Committee members and heads of various institutions in Nanjing went to the hospital to offer condolences. Feng Yuxiang, who arrived in Beijing from Tai'an on the 1st, also went to the hospital to visit after receiving the news. Representatives from various provinces and cities and overseas who came to Beijing to attend the Fifth National Congress were also heartbroken and went to the hospital to inquire about President Wang's condition. It is reported that the handgun used by the criminal was a four-inch Browning bullet. Although Wang was hit by three bullets, none were vital organs, and the injuries were not serious. There was no change in the afternoon. In addition to the Central Hospital's treatment, a plane was sent to Shanghai to bring bone specialist Niu Huilin to Beijing at 3:00 PM to assist in the treatment. The bullet in President Wang's back ribs was examined with an X-ray at around 3:00 PM. According to the doctor, President Wang's health will definitely not be in danger. (Central News Agency dispatch, 1st)

(Nanjing) After Shen Kefei and Liu Ruiheng used X-rays to examine the two bullets in President Wang's left cheek and back ribs, surgery was performed at around 4:00 PM to remove the bullet from the left cheek. During the surgery, Wang did not want to use anesthesia due to his strong physique, but because the incision was about an inch long, the area was slightly red and swollen. The bullet in the back ribs was embedded between the two ribs and was not easily removed at the time, but it was not a major issue. According to the doctor, it would not matter if it was not removed in the future. The surgery was completed after 5:00 PM, and Wang's spirits were still very good and he ate some fruit. According to the doctor's report at 10:00 PM, Wang's body temperature and pulse were still the same as when he was admitted to the hospital, with no changes. The previous telegram reported that Niu Huilin would come to Beijing, but it has been found to be misinformation. Chiang Kai-shek, Ye Chucang, Zhang Xueliang, and others visited the hospital again at 8:00 PM. (Central News Agency dispatch, 1st)

(Nanjing) President Wang's condition showed no change in the afternoon. At around 3:00 PM, X-rays were taken to examine the bullet wound in the shoulder and ribs. Feng Yuxiang arrived in Beijing and went to the hospital to visit Wang at 3:00 PM, but was unable to meet him because Wang was undergoing examination. Yu Youren, Shao Lizi, Liu Zhi, and dozens of others also went to the hospital to offer condolences after 3:00 PM, and were received by Zeng Zhongming. (Central News Agency dispatch, 1st)

(Nanjing) President Wang was shot a total of three times, once in the left cheek, once in the left arm, and once in the back ribs. He arrived at the Central Hospital at around 11:00 AM. According to the doctor's X-ray examination of the wound on his cheek, the bullet did not enter the bone, and was still in the skin outside the bone. The bullet had exited the wound on his left arm, without damaging the bones or blood vessels. The location of the bullet in the back ribs had not yet been found by X-ray. Because President Wang needs rest now, it is planned to examine it again in the afternoon. At present, President Wang is in good spirits and speaks clearly, but feels pain in his back and swelling under his left eyelid. According to doctors at the Central Hospital, Wang's injuries should not be a major problem. (Central News Agency dispatch, 1st)

No Change in Condition Late at Night

(Nanjing) Regarding President Wang's injuries, Central News Agency reporters went to the Central Hospital again at 12:00 AM on the 1st to visit. According to the doctor, President Wang's condition has not changed, and his pulse and body temperature are still the same as when he was admitted to the hospital. (Central News Agency dispatch, 1st)

Various Agencies to Conduct Strict Interrogation of Criminals Today

(Nanjing) The assassins arrested on the spot were the principal offender Sun Fengming and two accomplices, and four suspects. Except for Sun, who was sent to the hospital, the rest were sent to the police station. It was decided that on the 2nd, the main leaders of the Party, government, military, and police agencies would jointly conduct a strict interrogation. Sun is a reporter for Chenguang News Agency. After the incident, police officers immediately rushed to the agency to search it, but no one was found. Only many traces of burned documents were found in the stove, as well as remaining pieces of paper. Editorial manuscripts and other items were copied from the office and taken for research. This time, the Central Party Headquarters' restrictions on reporters entering and exiting were stricter than in the past, requiring a photo. The assassin went to collect the access pass on the 31st, but it was not complete, and he only received it on the morning of the 1st. During the 9:00 AM opening ceremony, reporters had to sign and match their photo when entering the venue. The criminal did not enter the auditorium, and no one expected that he would deliberately commit this outrageous act during the photography of the Central Committee members. (Central News Agency dispatch, 1st)

Chen Zhuo Says Criminal Was a Communist

(Nanjing) Regarding President Wang's assassination, Police Chief Chen Zhuo told Central News Agency reporters that the criminal in this case, Sun Fengming, had been interrogated and confessed that he was from outside the East Gate of Chuzhou, Anhui Province, 32 years old, and had served as a platoon leader in the 19th Route Army and a company commander of a machine gun company in the Mixed Regiment of the 12th Division of Fujian. He had been in Beijing for over a year, working as a reporter for Chenguang News Agency, and conspired with the agency's president Hu Yunqing and editor-in-chief He Poguang to assassinate President Wang for a long time. The revolver used in the assassination was given to him by Hu Yunqing, and the Central Propaganda Department's reporter access pass number 63 was obtained by He Poguang. Chenguang News Agency was registered by Hu Yunqing and others with the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau in October last year, originally located at 2 Wangheting Road, and later moved to 23 Lujia Lane. After this case occurred, the bureau sent police officers to the agency to search for the remaining members of the group, but all the personnel in the agency had already fled before the incident occurred, and all the documents had been burned in front of the stove. However, a letter was found on the desk with the words "Leave for those who come" written on the envelope, and the words "The affairs of this agency have nothing to do with Guo Zhimou, Wu Huang, and Zhou Xiling. We hereby declare" written on the note. The handgun seized on the spot was a Spanish-made six-shot revolver, gun number 8679. According to the criminal, it was purchased in Shanghai. All six bullets had been fired, and five empty shell casings were left on the cylinder. The reporter access pass worn by the criminal was introduced by Guo Zhimou to Wu Huang and Zhou Xiling, so they were able to obtain it from the Central Party Headquarters. According to the current investigation, the criminal and others deliberately planned the assassination, and their initial target was not just President Wang. The arrangements before and after the event were meticulously planned, making them undoubtedly communist bandits. The remaining members of the group are now being closely pursued in order to bring them to justice and punish them. Of the ten or more suspects apprehended today, some were those who acted hastily and did not heed police instructions during the incident at the Central Party Headquarters, and some were those who followed Chiang Kai-shek to and from the mausoleum this morning, acting suspiciously. The adjutant recorded their vehicle license plate numbers and notified them to be detained after the incident occurred. They are now being interrogated in detail in order to get to the bottom of the matter. (Central News Agency dispatch, 1st)

Wounded Worker's Bullet Has Been Removed

(Nanjing) The worker who was wounded by a stray bullet, named Zhu Hongjun, is Zhou Qigang's attendant. He was injured in the right foot. The bullet was removed by the Central Health Department and sent to Gulou Hospital for treatment. It will definitely not be a problem. (Central News Agency dispatch, 1st)

Zhang Ji Bravely Seized the Assassin

(Nanjing) According to official sources, Wang Jingwei was shot three times. The most serious bullet wound was in the back, penetrating the left lung. There were a total of three assassins. One was shot down by the guards and sent to the hospital. The other two fled into the Central Party Headquarters after the attack. The Party Headquarters was surrounded by military police. The two tried to resist arrest, but were eventually captured. Military police are now conducting a thorough search of the Party Headquarters to prevent any remaining members from hiding. According to witnesses, Zhang Ji bravely seized one of the assassins at the time, saving Wang's life. However, Zhang Ji was also hit by a bullet in the hand. (Reuters dispatch, 1st)

Assassin Also Sent to Central Hospital

(Nanjing) Today, during the opening ceremony of the Sixth Plenary Session, after the chairman gave a short speech, several photographers were taking photographs when suddenly an unknown person stepped forward and opened fire, injuring Wang. The assassin was shot down by the guards on the spot. After Wang was shot, the representatives rushed forward to help him into a car and sent him to the Central Hospital, where surgery was immediately performed to remove the bullet. The bullet was in the middle of the cheek. The assassin was also sent to the Central Hospital and underwent surgery. It is reported that his injuries are very serious. His name is still unknown. (Reuters dispatch, 1st)

(Nanjing) The assassin Sun Fengming refused to eat, so he was force-fed. (Special dispatch, 1st)

Current Commentary

Yesterday's Unfortunate Event in the Capital 2

— The Capital

Yesterday, after the Sixth Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee held its opening ceremony and the members had finished taking photographs, just as they were about to re-enter the venue, a sudden act of assassination took place. President Wang was shot three times and rushed to the Central Hospital for treatment. When the news spread, everyone was shocked and frightened. The local bond market even suspended trading because of this, indicating the severity of the matter. It is truly unprecedented in the capital for such a violent incident to occur at a grand event of the Central Party Headquarters, attracting nationwide attention, and with high-ranking Central officials in attendance. The impact of this event is significant enough to shake the world's attention and is not merely a major misfortune for the country.

The sudden occurrence of this incident has led to varied and speculative conjectures. Fortunately, all three perpetrators have been apprehended. Under thorough investigation, it will not be difficult to uncover the truth. Before the inside story is clarified, we are unwilling to make hasty comments. However, one point must be deeply lamented. Such an act of assassination is not something that can be carried out anywhere. At a time of serious national crisis, we depend on the sincere unity of all parties. The Sixth Plenary Session gathered leading figures together to jointly plan major national policies. Prior communication was not easy, and the people's expectations were high. However, this unexpected attack endangered the highest administrative official, increasing discord on national policies and providing an excuse for foreign powers. Therefore, this action by the thugs, whether driven by personal vendettas or acting as pawns with hidden backing, is an act against the world's conscience and should not be forgiven by public opinion. The dignitaries at the conference should maintain a calm attitude towards this sudden incident. On one hand, they should investigate the responsibility for the assassination, and on the other hand, continue the proceedings of the conference to prevent the discussion of proposals from being interrupted and to prevent the people's hearts from wavering, while waiting for President Wang's recovery. In addition to our extreme distress, we can only offer this humble contribution, hoping that the authorities will heed it.

(Continued from the fourth page of the first sheet)

Surgery Performed Without Anesthesia

(Nanjing) A certain important official left President Wang's bedside only at 11 o'clock tonight. According to reports, Wang is resting quietly. Surgery was performed this afternoon for two and a half hours without anesthesia, but with injections of Coramine. The injury to the left arm is not serious and can be treated easily, but the other two bullet wounds are more difficult. The bullet that entered the left cheek grazed a bone, causing fragments to fall into the left eye, so the left eye is now inflamed. After preliminary treatment, the doctor decided to wait until the inflammation subsides before performing further surgery tomorrow. The bullet that entered from the back passed between the sixth and seventh ribs, touching both ribs. The bullet is lodged in the flesh, but no internal organs were injured. (A Reuters dispatch dated the 1st)

Six Suspects Arrested

(Nanjing) Just after 10 o'clock this morning, after the opening ceremony of the Sixth Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee, when the members were gathered outside the conference hall for a photograph, gunshots suddenly rang out in succession, and President Wang was seen falling to the ground. There was chaos for a moment, and three people were seen holding smoking pistols, attempting to flee in a panic. However, the guards had already gathered and shot the leading assailant. During the commotion, two accomplices fled into the Central Party Headquarters. The building was immediately surrounded by military police. Subsequently, Zhang Xueliang led many people inside to capture them. Zhang himself also seized the weapon from one of them and kicked him to the ground. At the time of the incident, Chairman Chiang was in the auditorium of the Party Headquarters. Upon hearing the gunfire, he rushed out and helped Wang into a car to go to the hospital. Wang was hit by three bullets, one entering from the back and passing through the left rib, one hitting the left cheek, and one hitting the left arm. Blood gushed from his mouth. Shortly after, Chairman Chiang entered the hospital to visit him. Wang was able to speak. Chiang advised him not to speak and to rest quietly. After Wang entered the hospital, doctors performed surgery. According to a certain official who was watching, Wang's injuries are not as serious as initially feared. The motive for the attack has not yet been determined. The leading assailant, surnamed Sun, named Fengming, was also sent to the hospital for surgery. His injuries are said to be quite serious. He is about 20 years old, dressed in a Western suit with an overcoat. The weapon was hidden in the pocket of the overcoat. So far, six suspects have been arrested. The authorities are still searching the entire city for other accomplices. Sun has a Chenguang News Agency in Nanjing. After the incident, the police went to search the agency, but it was empty. The authorities have now taken strict measures to protect the members who have come to Nanjing to attend the meeting. Feng Yuxiang also arrived in Pukou this morning, and was greeted by He Yingqin and others. Only officials were allowed to enter the station at that time. News reporters who wanted to see Feng were refused. When the photograph was taken, the members were divided into five rows. Wang Jingwei, Yan Xishan, Zhang Xueliang, Zhang Ji, and others were in the front row. The assailant and his accomplices were mingled among the crowd of people near the cameras opposite the members. After the photograph was taken, as the members were about to return to the auditorium, the assailant rushed out of the crowd and shot Wang. Wang fell to the ground. Zhang Ji bravely rushed to the assailant and embraced him tightly from behind, but the assailant still fired seven or eight shots. Zhang Xueliang also rushed to help Zhang and kicked the assailant, who then fell to the ground and his weapon was seized. During the commotion, Wang's guards shot the assailant, and two accomplices took advantage of the chaos to mix into the crowd, but were eventually captured by Zhang Xueliang. Zhang Ji was not injured. In addition to Wang and the assailant, the only other person injured was a servant of the Party Headquarters, who was hit in the leg by a stray bullet and was not seriously injured. (A Reuters dispatch dated the 1st)

(Nanjing) It is now reported that the authorities have arrested a female suspect, young and beautiful, who speaks Russian fluently. She was formerly a member of the Chinese Communist Party, but has recently sworn allegiance to the Kuomintang. It is also reported that one person was arrested in Xiaguan. When arrested, he was reporting Wang's assassination over the phone. His clothing was similar to that of a plainclothes detective from the police department. A pistol was found on his person and confiscated. It is widely believed that this person is an accomplice of the Wang assassin. (A Reuters dispatch dated the 1st)

Executive Yuan Sends Telegram to the Capital to Express Condolences

(Hong Kong) The Executive Committee sent a telegram to the Central National Government in the capital on the 1st, stating that they were shocked to hear about the attack on Mr. Wang and Mr. Zhang. The comrades here are extremely horrified and request that condolences be conveyed and that details of the situation be telegraphed. (A special dispatch dated the 1st)

(Guangzhou) The Southwest Executive Committee and the Southwest Political Committee have jointly sent a telegram to the capital to express condolences to President Wang and others. Guangdong government leaders were greatly shocked upon hearing the news of Wang's assassination. They are now eagerly awaiting details of the case and are particularly concerned about Wang's injuries. (A Reuters dispatch dated the 1st)

London Circles Express Shock

(London) Tonight, all British newspapers have prominently published news of the assassination attempt on Wang Jingwei, the President of the Executive Yuan of China. All circles related to China have expressed deep shock and have unanimously praised Wang for his efforts for the country. At this time of national crisis, Mr. Wang is a rare and important figure in China, and it is deeply hoped that he will recover soon. Buckingham Palace and the Foreign Office expressed deep concern after receiving reports from Reuters. Viscount Cecil, President of the League of Nations Union, expressed deep sympathy and hopes for Wang's speedy recovery when interviewed by a Reuters reporter, saying, "Although I do not know Mr. Wang, all who know China recognize his value. China cannot be without this person in this difficult time." (A Reuters dispatch dated the 1st)

The Sixth Plenary Session Opened Yesterday; First Visited the Mausoleum to Pay Respects to the Late Premier's Remains; Solemn Opening Ceremony with Wang Delivering a Speech; Preparatory Meeting Elected the Presidium 3

(Nanjing) The Sixth Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee opened on the morning of the 1st. At 8:00 AM, the members of the Central Executive Committee first visited the Sun Yat-sen Mausoleum, including Chiang Kai-shek, Wang Zhaoming, Sun Ke, Yu Youren, Lin Sen, Cai Yuanpei, Dai Chuanxian, Yan Xishan, Zhang Xueliang, and over eighty others. Led by Chairman Lin Sen, they performed the rituals and laid wreaths. The entire group entered the mausoleum to pay respects to the late Premier's remains, and then took photographs. Afterwards, they returned to the Central Party Headquarters to hold the opening ceremony. The opening ceremony was held at 9:00 AM in the Central Auditorium. The auditorium was solemnly decorated, and the ceremony was very grand. Over one hundred members of the Central Executive Committee, representatives of various agencies, and staff members of the Party Headquarters, totaling over one thousand people, attended. Led by Chairman Wang Zhaoming, they performed the rituals and delivered the opening address. (The speech will be telegraphed separately.) The speech was very earnest and lasted for twenty minutes. Then, music was played and photographs were taken. At 10:30 AM, the preparatory meeting was held. One hundred and ten people attended. Only Wang Zhaoming was unable to attend due to his injuries. Yu Youren presided over the meeting. The resolutions were as follows: (1) To elect Chiang Kai-shek, Wang Zhaoming, Yu Youren, Sun Ke, Dai Chuanxian, Ding Weifen, and Ju Zheng as members of the Presidium of the Plenary Session; (2) To appoint Ye Chucang as the Secretary-General of the Plenary Session; (3) To establish a Proposal Review Committee. It was resolved that the Proposal Review Committee would be divided into five groups: Party Affairs, Politics, Military Affairs, Economy, and Education. The list of members for each group would be determined by the Presidium and reported to the General Assembly; (4) The Plenary Session would last for five days, starting from today; (5) Regarding the procedures for discussing proposals and the deadline, it was resolved that all proposals, except those submitted temporarily by the Presidium, would first be reviewed by the Proposal Review Committee and then submitted to the Presidium for consultation before being presented to the meeting. The deadline for receiving proposals was set at 12:00 PM on the evening of the 3rd; (6) To send representatives to express condolences to Committee Member Wang Zhaoming. It was resolved that Chiang Kai-shek, Kong Xiangxi, and Ye Chucang would be appointed as representatives to express condolences. (A Central News Agency dispatch dated the 1st)

First General Assembly to Be Held Today

(Nanjing) The Sixth Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee held a preparatory meeting on the morning of the 1st and rested in the afternoon. Original Text of Wang's Speech at the Plenary Session

(Nanjing) The original text of Wang Zhaoming's speech at the Plenary Session is as follows: "Comrades, since the Fifth Plenary Session was held, due to various reasons, the Sixth Plenary Session could only be held today. The number of committee members coming to the capital from various places is unprecedented, which fully demonstrates the fighting spirit of all comrades. This is very gratifying. Following the Sixth Plenary Session is the Fifth National Congress, so the Sixth Plenary Session is the conclusion of the Fourth National Congress and also the beginning of the Fifth National Congress. Therefore, this meeting is of great significance. We remember that when the Fourth National Congress was held, the nation was facing a serious crisis, so the slogan of the Fourth National Congress was 'Sincere Unity to Overcome the National Crisis.' Since the Fourth National Congress, from the First Plenary Session to today, all comrades have been working hard based on the meaning of 'Sincere Unity to Overcome the National Crisis.' We certainly dare not say that our efforts have achieved satisfactory results, but all previous plenary sessions have proceeded according to this direction. Now that the Fifth National Congress is approaching, the national crisis is even more serious than it was at the time of the Fourth National Congress. In the past few years, we have seen the efforts of all comrades, such as the efforts to suppress bandits, which have achieved great results, and other construction projects have also achieved some results. However, these achievements cannot give us satisfactory comfort because the national crisis has not been resolved and has become even more serious. We need to work harder and continue to work according to the direction set by the Fourth National Congress and contribute it to the Fifth National Congress. All kinds of work since the Fifth Plenary Session should be reported in detail at this plenary session, which I will not elaborate on first. Now, at the opening of the meeting, what I can report is that the spirit of sincere unity will never dissipate. Our heartache for the national crisis has increased our unlimited efforts. We are determined to bear this responsibility with unlimited courage and to seek a solution to the national crisis. We hope that based on this spirit and determination, this plenary session will obtain valuable discussions and valuable resolutions to be implemented." (A Central News Agency dispatch dated the 1st)

Feng Yuxiang Arrived from Tai'an

(Nanjing) Feng Yuxiang arrived in Beijing by special train from Tai'an at 11:30 AM on the 1st. He Yingqin, Zhu Peide, Zhang Ji, Li Liejun, Qin Zhen, Xue Dubi, He Chengjun, Liang Hancao, and over a hundred others all went to the Pukou Station to greet him. The station was under extremely strict guard. Feng got off the train, shook hands with the welcoming personnel to express his gratitude, and then took the Chengping ferry across the river to the city to rest. (A Central News Agency dispatch dated the 1st)

(Nanjing) Central Executive Committee member Feng Yuxiang arrived in Beijing at 11:30 AM on the 1st. Among those who went to welcome him were dozens of people, including Central Executive Committee members Zhang Ji, Li Liejun, Xue Dubi, and Tang Shengzhi. He is scheduled to attend the general assembly on the 2nd. When Mr. Feng arrived in Beijing, he was wearing a cloth short jacket and trousers, and black cloth shoes, and was in high spirits. After lunch, he went to visit Yan Xishan, the Director of the Pacification Headquarters of Shanxi Province. In the afternoon, he went to the Central Hospital to visit President Wang. Chairman Chiang visited Mr. Feng at the Lingyuan New Village in the afternoon after Mr. Feng arrived in Beijing. The meeting was very pleasant. Chiang left briefly to attend the plenary session and invited Mr. Feng to meet again in the evening. Mr. Feng brought important proposals with him on this trip, but whether they will be submitted for discussion at the plenary session will be decided after detailed consultation with the central authorities. (A special dispatch dated the 1st)

(Jinan) Zhu Jiqing and Enke Batu passed through Jinan by train this morning to go to Beijing to attend the Sixth Plenary Session. (A special dispatch dated the 1st)

Liu Xiang Supports the Sixth Plenary Session

(Chongqing) Liu Xiang telegraphed Beijing on the 31st, expressing support for the Sixth Plenary Session and offering two points of opinion: 1. Implement sincere unity; 2. Consolidate the center of gravity. (A special dispatch dated the 1st)

The Process of Convening the Sixth Plenary Session

(Nanjing) The process of convening the Sixth Plenary Session is as follows: According to the Party Constitution, the Central Plenary Session should be convened every six months. The Fifth Plenary Session was still convened in December of last year. In July of this year, the President of the Executive Yuan resigned. On August 1st, the 182nd Central Standing Committee meeting decided to convene the Sixth Plenary Session on September 20th. In early September, because the military campaign to suppress bandits had not yet been fully completed, the members of the Central Executive Committee who held military responsibilities were unable to come to Beijing, and the Fifth National Congress was also scheduled to be held on October 12th. The 187th Standing Committee meeting on September 5th resolved to postpone it to today. (A Central News Agency dispatch dated the 1st)

The Arrangement in front of the Sixth Plenary Session gate

After the Assassination Attempt on President Wang, the Executive Yuan Convened an Emergency Meeting 4

The Entire Group Went to the Hospital to Express Condolences and Vowed to Arrest the Culprits; It Was Also Resolved That Zhu Shaoliang Would Serve Exclusively in Military Positions in Gansu Province; Yu Xuezhong Appointed as Member and Chairman of the Gansu Provincial Government

(Nanjing) The Executive Yuan held an emergency meeting on the 1st, which was convened as a supplementary session at 3:00 PM. Kong Xiangxi, He Yingqin, Chen Shaokuan, Wang Shijie, Zhu Jiahua, and Chen Shuren attended. It was decided: (1) To go to the Central Hospital to express condolences to President Wang after the meeting; (2) To order the Ministry of Interior, the Ministry of Military Affairs, the Capital Police Department, and the Gendarmerie Command to strictly arrest the culprits; (3) To order the Capital Police Department and the Gendarmerie Command to pay special attention to security during the Central Executive Committee meeting; (4) To telegraph the provincial and municipal governments, informing them of the unfortunate incident that occurred this morning; (5) To appoint Zhu Shaoliang, the Director of the Pacification Headquarters of Gansu, to serve exclusively in military positions and to remove him from the concurrent position of Chairman of the Gansu Provincial Committee; and to appoint Yu Xuezhong as a member and Chairman of the Gansu Provincial Government. (A special dispatch dated the 1st)

(Nanjing) The Executive Yuan held an emergency meeting at 3:00 PM on the afternoon of the 1st. Kong Xiangxi, He Yingqin, Chen Shaokuan, Wang Shijie, Zhu Jiahua, Chen Shuren, and others attended, with Vice President Kong presiding over the meeting. The matters discussed were: (1) Resolved: The entire group will go to the Central Hospital to express condolences to President Wang; (2) Resolved: To order the Ministry of Interior, the Ministry of Military Affairs, the Capital Police Department, and the Gendarmerie Command to strictly arrest the culprit; (3) Resolved: To order the Capital Police Department and the Gendarmerie Command to pay special attention to security during the Central Executive Committee meeting; (4) Resolved: To telegraph the provincial and municipal governments, informing them of the unfortunate incident that occurred this morning; (5) Resolved: Zhu Shaoliang, Director of the Pacification Headquarters of Gansu, should serve exclusively in military positions and should be removed from the concurrent position of Chairman of the Gansu Provincial Government; Yu Xuezhong is appointed as a member and Chairman of the Gansu Provincial Government. (A Central News Agency dispatch dated the 1st)

(Nanjing) The regular meeting of the Executive Yuan next week was originally scheduled to be held one day earlier in the morning. Due to the assassination attempt on Wang, it was changed to 3:00 PM on the 1st. Vice President Kong presided over the meeting, which adjourned at 4:40 PM. All ministers and officials went to the Central Hospital to express condolences to President Wang. (A Central News Agency dispatch dated the 1st)

(Nanjing) After President Wang was assassinated, Chu Minyi, Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan, sent a telegram to the provinces and cities, reporting the incident. The original telegram is as follows: "To the Pacification Commissioners, the provincial and municipal governments, and the Weihaiwei Administration: Confidential. Today, after the opening ceremony of the Sixth Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee, Sun Fengming, a reporter from the Chenguang News Agency, suddenly opened fire on President Wang of this Yuan, injuring his left cheek, left arm, and back ribs in three places. He was immediately taken to the Central Hospital for treatment. After examination with X-rays, the doctors found that the bullet in his arm had been removed and had not injured any bones or nerves. The bullets in his cheek and back were both in the muscles. President Wang is currently in good spirits. According to the doctors at the Central Hospital, there should be no major problems. The assailant and his accomplices have already been arrested on the spot. Special notice is hereby given. Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan, Chu Minyi, east (day), west (day)." (A Central News Agency dispatch dated the 1st)

The Chairman of the Xingzhong Corporation Has Been Internally Decided 5

(Tianjin) The chairman of the Xingzhong Corporation has been internally decided to be Mr. Tohata, the former director of the South Manchuria Railway (Mantetsu). He is expected to arrive in Tianjin in mid-September. The capital amount is set at ten million, and will be increased to twenty million if necessary. A branch will be established in Shanghai. Mantetsu has decided to send Director Ishimoto and all the staff of the sixth section of the East Asia Department of Mantetsu to Tianjin on the 8th to assist the Xingzhong Corporation in economic planning. (A special dispatch dated the 1st)

(Tianjin) The Japanese industrial and political inspection group, consisting of Koshirou Inoue and twenty-three others, will arrive in Tianjin from Tanggu at 8:20 PM on the 1st. They are scheduled to visit Commander Tada at 9:00 AM on the 2nd. At 10:00 AM, they will attend a tea party, symposium, and lecture meeting organized by various circles in Tianjin at Nankai University. On the 3rd, they will tour the city and visit the shrine before going to Beiping. (A special dispatch dated the 1st)

(Tianjin) The Japanese-Manchu-Mongolian Woolen Fabric Company is establishing a branch in Tianjin with a capital of two million. The annual turnover is targeted at eight million. Preparations have been completed. Purchasing operations will begin on the 15th, and the factory will be built next spring. (A special dispatch dated the 1st)

(Tianjin) Mantetsu dispatched eight senior employees to Tianjin on the 1st: Itsutsugi Nishimura, Tadao Sakaguchi, Ichimasa Tanaka, and Naritoku Matsu. They will prepare for the economic cooperation organization, the Xingzhong Corporation. The company has already rented the entire fifth floor of the Xinhua Building on No. 4 Road in the Tianjin Concession, totaling over two hundred rooms. The Tianjin Mantetsu office will also be located there and is scheduled to move in next week, with operations starting around the 30th. The capital is ten million, with one-quarter of the capital being raised first. The Tianjin portion of the capital is being raised by Gao Lingyu, Niu Chuanshan, and others. (A special dispatch dated the 1st)

Domestic and Foreign Telegrams Began to Be Sent and Received Yesterday 6

(Tianjin) Direct telegrams between inside and outside the customs and the sending and receiving of Japanese telegrams began on the morning of the 1st. It has been quite smooth. There have been quite a few incoming and outgoing telegrams. Japanese telegrams cost 12 cents per word, with each five characters counted as one word. Cipher telegrams cost 24 cents per word. News telegrams cost 3 cents per word. Urgent regular telegrams cost twice as much as regular telegrams. Urgent news telegrams cost the same as regular telegrams. (A special dispatch dated the 1st)

(Tianjin) At noon on the 1st, one company each of Japanese artillery and engineers arrived in Tianjin from Japan, increasing their strength. Japanese military attaché to Jinan, Yoshio Ishino, arrived in Tianjin to meet with Tada to make some requests. (A special dispatch dated the 1st)

Today, he will take the afternoon train to Guangdong, then to Guangxi. He will return to Hong Kong around the 6th or 7th and return to Japan on the Hakusan Maru. (A special dispatch dated the 1st)

Page 7

League of Nations Sanctions Awaiting Implementation; Anglo-French Negotiations Reach Impasse; Basis for Peaceful Resolution Difficult to Establish, Three-Party Contact Still Intended to Continue 9

(Geneva) Peace negotiations have reached an impasse. While all parties are prepared to negotiate, they face the difficulty of not knowing where to start. A key figure in the British delegation stated today that although French Foreign Minister Laval and British Foreign Secretary Hoare have met, there is still no hope of a resolution. (1st, National News Agency)

(Geneva) Hoare, Eden, and Laval held talks today for an hour and a half. Both the British and French sides described the talks as fruitful. Laval is scheduled to meet with Italian representative Aloisi this afternoon. It is expected that Laval will issue a statement tomorrow regarding the recent talks in Paris, indicating that a solid basis for a resolution has not yet been established. (1st, Reuters)

(Geneva) According to a spokesman for the central delegation, Foreign Secretary Hoare and Minister Without Portfolio Eden met with French Prime Minister Laval this morning from 11:30 AM to 12:30 PM. It was immediately decided to request the Sanctions Committee to specify the earliest possible date for the implementation of sanctions. When the Sanctions Committee meets in the afternoon, Laval or Hoare will present a report on the aims and achievements of recent British and French diplomatic activities, explaining that although a compromise has not yet been reached on a solution, the British and French governments have decided to continue their efforts to find such a solution. Experts from the British and French delegations are currently engaged in discussions in Paris to find a basis for negotiations, and will come to Geneva as soon as results are achieved. Representatives from the British and French governments are also scheduled to continue discussions in the afternoon. In addition, Laval will meet with Italian representative Aloisi and Belgian Prime Minister Theunis this afternoon. British Foreign Secretary Hoare is scheduled to return to London tomorrow, while Laval is scheduled to leave for Paris tomorrow afternoon or Sunday morning. (1st, Havas)

(Geneva) British Foreign Secretary Hoare arrived here at 10:00 AM this morning. He met with French Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval in the morning. Italian government representative Aloisi will not arrive until 4:30 PM this afternoon. Regarding the resolution of the Italian-Abyssinian dispute, although there has been some negotiation between Britain and France, there is little hope of a compromise between the two countries. According to the suggestions made by British expert Peterson and French expert Saint-Quentin in Paris, the Italian viewpoint would be given much consideration. However, the British government opposes dividing Abyssinian territory into metropolitan and non-Amharic provinces, placing these provinces under Italian control, and giving Italy a leading role in the implementation of international aid programs in central Abyssinia. League of Nations officials believe that Britain will continue to maintain this stance until before the implementation of sanctions on November 14. On the French side, it is said that French Prime Minister Laval still advocates taking prompt action to mediate the dispute before implementing sanctions, so as not to create unnecessary complications in the already tense situation. However, it is unlikely that a solution to the dispute will be reached in the current meeting of the Sanctions Committee. The Sanctions Committee will decide on the date of implementation of sanctions tomorrow. This date will likely be between November 10 and November 15. The diplomatic representatives of various countries will remain in Geneva for no more than two days. (1st, Havas)

(Geneva) The French representatives here are quite optimistic about the situation, hoping that reconciliation can ultimately be achieved. However, the British representatives do not share this view. They declared today that the Anglo-French talks last week achieved nothing and are not enough to promote peace, and therefore advocate for strict sanctions. (1st, National News Agency)

(Rome) A foreign ministry spokesman said that Italy does not intend to propose a solution to the Italian-Abyssinian dispute in Geneva, but can study any concessions made by other countries. Anyone who believes that Italy can accept any solution that harms its dignity and interests due to pressure from League of Nations sanctions is greatly mistaken. (31st, National News Agency)

(Geneva) The Sanctions Committee reconvened today to consider reports from member states on their plans regarding Italy. The reports stated that 50 countries have agreed to the proposal to ban arms exports to Italy, 49 countries have agreed to ban financial loans, and 48 countries have agreed to ban Italian imports. After considering the report, the committee decided to reconvene after the Committee of Eighteen determines the date of implementation of sanctions against Italy. (31st, Reuters)

(Geneva) The League of Nations Council met today to discuss the date for implementing sanctions against Italy. The Committee of Eighteen is now ready to decide on a date to completely boycott Italian goods and prohibit the sale of major products to Italy. It is also reported that after adjourning this Saturday, the Sanctions Committee will reconvene within a month to consider the possibility of withdrawing ambassadors and ministers from various countries and ending travel to Italy as the fourth step in sanctions. The Sanctions Committee will thank the United States for expressing its sympathy for the League of Nations. (31st, National News Agency)

Date of Sanctions Can Be Decided Imminently; Only Debt Poses Some Problems 10

(Geneva) The various subcommittees dealing with the issue of sanctions against Italy will meet here this morning. It is expected that the implementation of the arms embargo and financial sanctions will not be delayed. However, the subcommittee dealing with contracts and liquidation of contracts has encountered some difficulties. At yesterday's meeting of the Committee of Eighteen, the Romanian representative stated that Italy owed Romania a substantial amount of money and that he could not agree to the date of implementation of sanctions until this problem was resolved. However, a compromise may be reached regarding the issue of Italy's ultimate repayment of the debt. The date of implementation of economic sanctions may be decided today or tomorrow. (1st, Reuters)

(Geneva) The Committee of Eighteen continued its meeting this afternoon, resolving to entrust the legal and financial committees to study the replies from various countries regarding the arms embargo and financial sanctions. The committees are scheduled to meet tomorrow. The subcommittee then continued to discuss whether the part of pre-existing purchase contracts between various countries and Italy that had not yet been fulfilled should also be subject to sanctions. It was decided that the economic sanctions subcommittee should study the situation in each country separately. (31st, Havas)

(Geneva) The Indian government today notified the League of Nations that it was willing to support in principle the sanctions against Italy decided by the League of Nations in accordance with Article 16, paragraph 3, of the Covenant. However, the extent to which it can implement such sanctions depends on the extent to which other countries willing to take the same action respect Indian trade and absorb Indian raw materials that have stopped being shipped to Italy. (31st, Reuters)

Dublin The administrative leader of the Irish Free State, de Valera, today introduced a League of Nations obligations bill in the Dáil, stipulating the immediate implementation of sanctions against Italy and assistance to League of Nations member states taking the same action. If this bill is not opposed within 21 days, it will become law. (31st, Reuters)

(Geneva) Egypt today notified the League of Nations that it is willing to abide by the principles of implementing economic and financial sanctions against the Italo-Abyssinian conflict, and will implement the plan resolved by the League of Nations to the extent possible. The League of Nations considers this resolution important because Egypt is the only non-member state that has now fully accepted all sanctions. (31st, Reuters)

(Paris) Italy today began a counteroffensive against the League of Nations sanctions, refusing to renew the reciprocal tariffs on Franco-Italian wines. From this afternoon, all French wines imported into Italy will be subject to full tariffs. Several special trains loaded with raw materials and food are heading into Italy, demonstrating Italy's concern about the sanctions. France is still buying Italian goods, but the government has banned the export of aircraft engines ordered by General Balbo of Italy in September. (31st, National News Agency)

Roosevelt's Declaration Arouses Various Speculations 11

Banning General Trade is Beyond the President's Authority

(Washington) President Roosevelt and Secretary of State Hull issued a declaration yesterday, advising the American people not to trade with warring nations. This has aroused considerable speculation today. It is unknown whether the nature of this declaration is merely an encouragement to the League of Nations in passing, or a disguised warning, stating that the United States is actually considering legal steps to ban the supply of goods to the people of warring nations. Legal experts here are divided on whether the President has the power to ban general trade. Some experts believe that when the Neutrality Act was passed, Congress only specifically mentioned cotton as being exempt from any ban, so the President can ban the export of other goods. However, some experts say that although the Neutrality Act affects war materials, banning general trade is beyond the President's authority. (31st, National News Agency)

Mediterranean Naval Reduction Issue; Anglo-Italian Negotiations Unresolved; Some Difficulties Have Arisen 12

(London) It was learned from reliable sources today that Britain has decided to keep its fleet stationed in the Mediterranean, pending improvement in relations with Italy. It was also learned that French naval experts currently in London are discussing the specific ways in which France would assist Britain in the event of hostilities in the Mediterranean. It is reported here that British Ambassador to Italy Drummond informally told Mussolini that Britain cannot reduce its three-fleet concentration in the Mediterranean until Italian newspapers and radio stations cease their attacks on Britain and until Italian forces in Libya are reduced to normal levels. (31st, National News Agency)

(London) According to reliable sources today, Italian Prime Minister Mussolini has notified Britain that he cannot recognize Britain's maintenance of its current naval strength in the Mediterranean as a self-defense action. According to authoritative reports, when Mussolini met with British Ambassador to Italy Drummond on Wednesday, the Italian Prime Minister took note of Britain's refusal to reduce its Mediterranean fleet in response to Italy's withdrawal of its troops from Libya. Although Mussolini does not regard Britain's current naval strength as an act of aggression, he told the British Ambassador that Britain's refusal to reduce its troops is an inexplicable anti-Italian action. (31st, National News Agency)

Roman Pope Advocates Placing Abyssinia Under Italian Mandate; To Avoid More Dangerous War 13

(Rome) Pope Pius XI today strongly urged various countries to place Abyssinia under Italian mandate "to avoid a more dangerous war." Prior to this, the Pope had notified the bishops of Rome that the sanctions imposed by the League of Nations have no relation to the Vatican or the monasteries here. All import debts or credits of church institutions are not hindered. It is learned that the Pope's attitude will be detailed in an editorial in the Catholic newspaper "Catholic Culture." The editorial will openly advocate that the League of Nations should immediately place Abyssinia under Italian mandate without further hesitation in order to prevent a more serious conflict in Europe or the world. The reason cited by the newspaper for Italy's mandate over Abyssinia is that after the European War, various countries obtained many German territories, but Italy alone had none. The newspaper will also ask Catholics in Britain and France to strive to understand Italy's needs. Observers also believe that the Pope has now instructed his representative in France, Maglione, to find ways to persuade French Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval to do his best to obtain British agreement to this proposal. (31st, National News Agency)

Fierce Battles Erupt on Southern Front; Abyssinian Troops Courageously Resist Powerful Enemy 14

More Than 3,000 Killed and Wounded; Commander Killed; Italian Troops on Northern Front Advance Towards Magale

(London) According to news from Addis Ababa, the capital of Abyssinia, the Italian troops on the northern front occupied the town of Makele this morning. (1st, National News Agency)

(London) The situation in Magale is currently chaotic. According to news from Addis Ababa, Italian troops have occupied the city, but this claim has not been verified in Rome. Italian sources say that the Abyssinian leader Gufsa, who surrendered to Italy, heard that the government had offered a reward of 50,000 Abyssinian dollars for his head. He is now leading his troops to attack Magale. General Gaza, the commander of the Abyssinian army on the northern front, has destroyed all of his property in Magale. At 6:00 AM on Monday, 1,600 men set out to attack the city. No news has been heard since. Rome is now hoping that this force has captured the city. (1st, Reuters)

(Rome) The Ministry of the Army announced today that the vanguard of the Italian troops on the northern front, commanded by General De Bono, military governor of Eritrea, has now approached Makele. (31st, National News Agency)

(Paris) A newspaper here received a cable today from its correspondent in Addis Ababa stating that Abyssinian troops suffered 3,500 casualties in recent battles near the Wogadaen line. The fighting around Waller was extremely fierce, and Abyssinian troops failed to capture the area. Abyssinian troops are resisting the heavily armed enemy with exceptional courage. Their commander, Abate Kemeir, is reported to have been killed in action. (31st, Reuters)

Addis Ababa According to private sources, fierce battles have taken place recently in several places on the Wogadaen front. Abyssinian troops near Waller Waller suffered heavy attacks and failed to succeed. The Abyssinian commander, Kemeir, was killed in action during this battle, and there were 3,500 other casualties. The Italian trenches are very well constructed. The Abyssinian troops resisted heroically, and the fighting was very intense. (31st, Havas)

Harar War correspondents arriving here today reported that fighting on the southern front is still quite active, but it appears that there has been little progress in the main offensive by Abyssinian troops. Reinforcements have been dispatched to Gora Hae today, which is still in Abyssinian hands. However, there is no news of the great victory hoped for by the general public. According to the situation in the provincial headquarters, the so-called large-scale offensive has failed in both the south-east and south-west after minor setbacks in Qeqe. (31st, National News Agency)

Asmara According to news received here today, Italian troops on the northern front are gradually advancing towards Magale from various areas. It is reported that the troops of General Santini have occupied the Me Yuk Well, ten miles from Atgamus. The Second Army Corps, attacking on the right wing, is reported to have advanced seven miles towards El Aqing on the border with British-Egyptian Sudan. In order to prevent Abyssinian troops from flanking the extreme right on the northern front, Italian troops have now established defenses along the Setit River, using machine guns to await the enemy. The Italian troops attacking Magale on the left wing are also taking the same precautions, building numerous small forts along the watershed to prevent Abyssinian troops from flanking from the Danakil area. (31st, Reuters)

Italian Troops Attacked

Addis Ababa The authorities here announced today that the fierce Danakil tribesmen twice raided Italian troops at night, heavily damaging Italian troops near Mount Mousa Ali. The tribe attacked a military supply vehicle, killing 15 Italian soldiers. The second attack targeted an Italian infantry artillery unit and a tank unit advancing westward from Mengala through the wilderness. The enemy suffered heavy casualties. The Abyssinians today firmly believe that the Italians are planning to build an airfield near Alaqla. 15,000 Italian regular troops and soldiers are concentrated west of Mount Mousa Ali. A spokesman for the Abyssinian emperor declared today that the Italians will definitely not be able to cross the desert. If the Italian troops continue to advance, there will be many deaths. (31st, National News Agency)

Italian Special Forces Active

Front Line in Italian Somaliland News from our correspondent indicates that the Italian "Dubat" special forces recently launched an attack on the enemy troops northwest of Marcal, killing 11 enemy soldiers. Three soldiers of the "Dubat" special forces were also killed in action and two were wounded. At that time, the enemy troops also planned to attack the special forces. Although the "Dubat" special forces treated them with friendship, the tribe unexpectedly opened fire first, and the Italian special forces also retaliated. This is the situation of the conflict between the two sides. (1st, Havas)
