The main goal of the work is to enable the citizens in the area to follow the measures for practicing a new life promulgated by the bureau, item by item, and put them into practice, so that the promotion of the New Life Movement will not become empty talk on paper. Those who do not comply after being advised will be warned. Those who repeatedly resist and refuse to comply after being warned will be punished in accordance with the Regulations on Punishment of Violations of Police Regulations.

China Merchants Bureau: The Issue of Ship Crew Deducting for Disaster Relief has been Resolved 97

First Deducting One-Quarter of Monthly Salary, Then Another One-Quarter Next Month

According to Guomin News Agency, the misunderstanding caused by the issue of deducting salary for disaster relief among all crew members of the state-run China Merchants Bureau has been resolved. The two labor unions of the local marine engineers and captains sent a letter to the bureau, stating that they were willing to deduct half a month's salary from the double salary savings of each person over the years to pay for the disaster relief fund. Since the end of October has passed and the bureau is about to pay wages and deduct for the disaster relief fund, the representatives of the marine engineers' union, Feng Yuming, together with the representatives of the bureau's labor union, You Zhijun, Zheng Xuliang, etc., met with Liu Hongsheng yesterday morning to request that half a month's salary be withdrawn from the savings as a disaster relief fund to avoid affecting the economy of the crew members and workers. Liu Hongsheng persuaded the three representatives, saying that the deduction for disaster relief was determined by the ministry and commission, and the bureau was not in a position to violate the measures. As for the double salary savings, he himself could be responsible for raising a part of the cash and then submitting it to the ministry for approval to be issued to everyone. This would not hinder the lives and economy of each person. Now, one-quarter of the monthly salary will be deducted first, and another one-quarter will be deducted next month. A dispute has finally been resolved.

Affected by Gold Prices, the Silk Ribbon and Electric Bulb Industries Have Increased Prices 99

Importers of woolen cloth and other goods must pay in cash; exporters of silk, tea, and other goods are buying in large quantities.

Due to the recent soaring gold prices, the prices of imported goods have also increased accordingly. The silk ribbon and electric bulb industries have issued notices of price increases. Details are as follows:

Silk Ribbon Industry

The local silk ribbon industry association has recently been affected by the rise in gold prices and the fall in silver prices, causing the price of rayon to soar. The original selling price is difficult to maintain. A special notice has been issued stating that prices will be increased by 20% starting from November 1st. The notice states: "Dear colleagues, due to the impact of the recent rise in gold prices and the fall in silver prices, the cost of raw materials has risen sharply. If we continue to sell at the old prices, it will be difficult to maintain. Therefore, we have convened a special meeting and decided that all goods will increase in price by 10% starting from November 1st to maintain our capital and make up for our losses. We hope that all dealers will understand."

Electric Bulb Industry

Electric bulb factories have also issued notices of a 10% price increase. The original text states: "Dear colleagues, our factories have been manufacturing electric bulbs for years. We have been affected by the downturn in the market, and due to the competition among colleagues, the selling price has been falling, and we have been suffering deeply. In recent years, we have also encountered a shortage of raw materials, and prices have been soaring, increasing our costs. The selling price is still the same as before, and we must purchase raw materials in cash, while wholesale electric bulbs are mostly sold on credit. Our situation is even more difficult than before. Although our factories have been struggling to support ourselves, we feel that there are hidden dangers. If we do not seek remedies urgently, the consequences will be unthinkable. Therefore, we have gathered colleagues from all over Shanghai to discuss solutions. We have unanimously agreed on the following articles, and we hope that all customers from home and abroad will understand and appreciate them: (1) Starting from November 1st of this year, the selling price will be increased by 10% across the board. (2) All goods sold will not be exchanged. (3) Accounts must be settled at the end of each month, and the outstanding amount must be paid in full in order to facilitate turnover. Checks are limited to ten days."

Imports and Exports

European and American foreign firms importing goods are suspending orders due to the instability of foreign exchange rates, and merchants such as paint dealers have been requiring cash payments since last month. Other imported goods such as woolen cloth, machinery, textiles, and miscellaneous goods also require cash payments. Due to the gold price situation, exporters are also buying in large quantities. Sales of tea, silk, eggs, and other goods have been strong recently, and prices have also soared accordingly.

Municipal Central Detective Squad Solves Murder Case, Arrests Perpetrators 105

Jin Miaosheng, Jin Mao Da, Tao Rongsheng, Three Men

Previously, Gao Xuan, a poor Shandong scavenger in Wangjiabang, Songhu Road, Jiangwan, was beaten to death by local residents Jin Miaosheng, Jin Fufu, Jin Tisheng, and Jin Furong. The case was reported to the Shanghai Local Court for investigation and arrest of the murderers. However, the suspects had absconded, making it impossible to apprehend them for a time. Later, the court issued official letter No. 302 to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for their arrest. At the same time, the Central Detective Squad also received Instruction No. 102705 from the Public Security Bureau Headquarters, stating in brief: "According to the complaint submitted by Cai Mengwu, his cousin Gao Xuan was murdered for no reason, requesting strict apprehension of the murderers and prosecution according to law." Therefore, after the case occurred, Ji Yuanpu and Wang Huibai, the captain and deputy captain of the Public Security Bureau Detective Corps, immediately instructed Wu Kezhong and Chu Jingwu, the captain and deputy captain of the Central Detective Squad, to conduct a thorough investigation. Until about 1:00 PM on the 31st of last month, Detective Cao Maosheng learned that the murderer Jin Miaosheng was going to Jiangwan for a wedding banquet. Captains Wu and Chu, upon receiving the report, immediately led leaders Wang Yao and Bao Guanwu, detective Cao Maosheng, and police officers dispatched by the Jiangwan Police Station to a small teahouse opened by a Gao family on Xinshi Road to lie in wait. Shortly after, Jin Miaosheng arrived and was apprehended. However, after the incident, his father, Jin Zigao, and Jin Fufu's father, Jin Miaoqing, entrusted a person named Ma Changshu to settle the matter, spending a total of 7-800 yuan. Later, Jin Mao Da and Tao Rongsheng brought 300 yuan. Because I had no money, I mortgaged 1.8 mu of land for 70 yuan. Jin Tisheng took out 80 yuan, and Jin Fufu and Jin Furong contributed 150 yuan together. On October 5th, Jin Mao Da and Tao Rongsheng sent three copies of a newspaper, saying that our matter had been settled and published in the newspaper, telling us to rest assured. After receiving the confession, the squad dispatched Tao Jinsen, Peng Jie, and others to Jiangwan and Wangjiabang to arrest the suspects, apprehending Jin Mao Da and Tao Rongsheng. Their confessions were very cunning. Jin Fufu, Jin Ti Quan, and Jin Shi have all fled upon hearing the news. The squad then handed over the arrest warrant and the suspects Jin Miaosheng, extortionist Jin Mao Da, and Tao Rongsheng to the Central Branch Bureau. Director Huang Liuguang immediately dispatched officer Zhang Lourong to interrogate them. Yesterday afternoon, they were sent to the Public Security Bureau Headquarters for interrogation.

Forced Solicitation of Prostitution Fees Leads to Fatal Fall 106

Xu Dawu, Mute Zhongyan Flees; Two Women and Paramours Arrested

Xu Dawu, a 36-year-old from Changzhou who set up fortune-telling stalls, and his colleague, Mute Zhongyan (the business name, real name unknown), 26 years old, checked into room number five of the Lixing Inn at 341 Avenue Foch (near the slaughterhouse) in the French Concession on the 28th of last month. During the day, the two went out separately to conduct business. On the evening of the 31st, they went to the Tianyun Building on the roof of Wing On Company, where they met female attendants Li Xiuying (33 years old, from Haimen) and Wu Gendi (31 years old, from Ningbo). The two women lived together at No. 34, Shangyi Lane, Xiaocai Field, Rue du Père Robert, French Concession. Li had an affair with Zhang Fusheng, 31 years old, from Haining, and Wu had an affair with Chen Yongxing, 29 years old, from the same hometown. They lived in adjacent rooms. The two women struck up a conversation, quickly becoming inseparable. In fact, the two women were prostitutes. Xu and Mute took Li and Wu back to the Lixing Inn for illicit relations. Xu and Li stayed in the original room number five, while Mute and Wu opened another room, number eight. Upon arriving at the inn, the two women immediately demanded prostitution fees. Xu and others replied that they had eighty yuan deposited in the inn's accounting office, but the accountant was not present at the moment. They would retrieve it in the morning and pay the full amount without shortage. Li and Wu, seeing Xu and Mute dressed in Western suits and appearing wealthy, did not suspect a trick and believed them. They each returned to their rooms. Little did they know that overnight, the two women got up at 7 am and asked Xu and Mute for the prostitution fees. To their surprise, Xu and others had no money at all. The agreement made the previous night was purely a deception. The two women were furious and started arguing. Mute seized the opportunity to escape without a trace. Li Xiuying kept Xu Dawu from leaving. Wu Gendi went home to call her and Li’s paramours, Zhang Fusheng and Chen Yongxing. They gathered several hoodlums and rushed to Lixing Inn, where they questioned Xu, demanding the prostitution fees. Seeing the disparity in numbers, Xu felt trapped and jumped out of the window of room five on the third floor to escape. He fell to the ground, crushing the back of his head, bleeding profusely, and dying instantly. The inn's tea boy discovered the incident and detained Li and Wu, as well as Zhang and Chen. They reported the incident to the French police, who dispatched detectives to investigate and took the two women and two men to the police station for questioning. The body was transported to the Tongren Fuyuan branch hall for examination. It is scheduled to be reported to the court for inspection today.

Full Text of Gu Zhuxuan's Judgment 110

Investigating whether the defendant instigated the murder of Tang, referring to the Supreme Court's judgment date. Gu handed over a pistol and adopted Zhang Tinggui's confession. Xue Zhenyi's three letters to Zheng Qian can prove it.

Gu Zhuxuan, the former head of the Zhabei Security Corps, the president of the Jianghuai Fellow Villagers Association in Shanghai, and the owner of the Tianchan Theater, a native of Fallen City, Jiangsu, in June of the 22nd year of the Republic [1933], instigated Wang Xinggao, Zhao Guangfu, Zhang Tinggui, and the fugitive Zhou the Carpenter, etc., to assassinate Tang Jiapeng, the manager of the Great World, resulting in his death. At the same time, a passerby, Wu Guangcai (a native of Yangzhou, working as a waiter in a bathhouse, whose coffin and burial expenses were paid by the Tang family after his death, and his remains were claimed by his family), was killed by a stray bullet. The crime was reported by the felon Zhao Guangfu to the Law Enforcement Department. On September 10th, Gu was arrested by the French Concession Police and sent to the Second Special Court, where he was prosecuted for the crime of instigating murder. After repeated trials by Judge Wang Wangxu, accompanied by Assessors Xiong Huiping and Zhang Chaozuo, who together confirmed that Gu had committed the crime, on the 28th of last month, a judgment was pronounced sentencing Gu Zhuxuan to fifteen years of imprisonment and ten years of deprivation of civil rights. During the appeal period, he was remanded to the detention center and temporarily detained at the Guangci Hospital. All the details have been recorded in this newspaper. The judgment has been sent to the police station, and we have looked for and recorded it.

The full text of the judgment is as follows: Criminal Judgment No. 334, Jiesu, of the Jiangsu Shanghai Second Special District Local Court, the twenty-fourth year of the Republic [1935]. Judgment against the defendant Gu Zhuxuan, male, age fifty, native of Yancheng, occupation merchant, residing at No. 9, Yonghe Lane, No. 222, North Xizang Road, elected defense attorneys Wu Kaisheng, Xue Dubi, and Lin Dawen. The above-mentioned defendant was prosecuted by the French Concession Police Department for the case of instigating murder. This court, after hearing the case, makes the following judgment:

Main text: Gu Zhuxuan is sentenced to fifteen years of imprisonment for instigating murder and ten years of deprivation of civil rights.

Facts: Gu Zhuxuan harbored resentment towards Tang Jiapeng, the former manager of the Great World Amusement Park. In June of the 22nd year of the Republic [1933], he ordered Wang Xinggao, also known as Wang Jinkui, to secretly invite people to find a way to kill him. Wang Xinggao first booked Room 208 on the second floor of the Asia Hotel on Avenue Edward VII as a meeting place. On June 12th, Wang Xinggao and Zhou Qifu went to Hengfeng Road in Zhabei and invited Zhang Tinggui, also known as Zhang Xiaosizi, to participate, explaining that this was Gu Zhuxuan's matter and there was no need to be afraid. They also instructed him to invite others. Zhang Tinggui then invited Gu Dengyang and Zhou the Carpenter (also known as Zhou Mingxiang) to join. On the afternoon of June 13th, at around 10:00 PM, Zhou Qifu invited Zhang Tinggui to Room 208 of the Asia Hotel. Gu Zhuxuan also arrived at the location. After Gu Zhuxuan and Wang Xinggao had a private conversation, Gu took out two pistols and handed them to Wang Xinggao and left. At around 9:00 AM on June 16th, Zhou the Carpenter went to Datong Road in Zhabei and invited Zhao Guangfu, explaining that Gu Zhuxuan wanted to kill his enemy and invited him to participate. After Zhao Guangfu agreed, Zhou the Carpenter invited him to the Renhe Teahouse in Xinqiao, where he met with Wang Xinggao. Wang Xinggao and Zhou the Carpenter then invited Zhao Guangfu to Room 208 on the second floor of the Asia Hotel. Shortly after, Gu Zhuxuan entered the room and said that the manager of the Great World was his enemy and told them to do it without worry. It was then decided that Gu Dengyang and Zhao Guangfu would carry out the deed, Zhang Tinggui would act as a lookout, and Wang and Gao's grandson would deliver the pistols. Zhang Tinggui was also instructed to scout out Tang Jiapeng's daily arrival time from the Great World. On the night of June 16th, 22nd year of the Republic [1933], they waited together at the entrance of the Great World to kill Tang Jiapeng, but they did not encounter him. The next afternoon, at around 11:00 PM, Zhang Tinggui and others went to the location and waited according to the original plan. At 1:20 AM (that is, the morning of June 18th), they saw Tang Jiapeng walking out of the entrance of the Great World and getting into a car. Gu Dengyang opened fire, and Zhao Guangfu also fired three shots at him. Tang Jiapeng died shortly after being shot. Wu Guangcai, who was walking on the road, was also wounded and killed by stray bullets. Both were examined by the court's forensic doctor, who confirmed that they died from gunshot wounds and attached the autopsy report to the file. Afterwards, Zhang Tinggui received 60 yuan and fled to the countryside. Zhao Guangfu was detained for keeping the pistol and had not yet received his money. On November 28th of the same year, he was arrested by the police department. Zhang Tinggui also filed a lawsuit against Zhao Guangfu in the First Special District Local Court, and this court sentenced Zhao Guangfu to life imprisonment and Zhang Tinggui to 20 years in prison. While the case was being appealed to the Supreme Court, Zhao Guangfu, due to not receiving his reward and being imprisoned, reported Wang Xinggao to the police department in December of last year. Wang Xinggao was arrested by the police department, and this court sentenced him to life imprisonment for the crime of instigating murder. In July of this year, Zhao Guangfu sued Gu Zhuxuan in this court for instigating murder. After this court issued a judgment of non-acceptance, he reported the previous situation to the police department. After Gu Zhuxuan was arrested and interrogated by the police department, he was prosecuted in court according to Article 29 and Article 271 of the Criminal Law.

Reason: Tang Jiapeng, the former manager of the Great World, was indeed shot and killed by Zhao Guangfu and Gu Dengyang. This has been confirmed by the criminal judgment of Zhao Guangfu and Zhang Tinggui, also known as Zhang Xiaosizi. What should be investigated now is whether the defendant in this case actually instigated Zhao Guangfu, Zhang Tinggui, and others to kill Tang Jiapeng. After repeated interrogations by this court, although the defendant firmly refused to confess, attempting to evade criminal responsibility, according to Zhao Guangfu's confession, Tang Jiapeng was killed by Zhou the Carpenter, that is, Zhou Mingxiang, who found me in Zhabei at Hengfeng Road at seven or eight o'clock in the morning on June 16th, 22nd year of the Republic [1933], to have tea. After having tea, we went to the Renhe Teahouse to have tea. Wang Xinggao also came to the Renhe Teahouse. They said that it was the matter of Fourth Master Gu. From the Renhe Teahouse, we went to Room 208 of the Asia Hotel. Gu Zhuxuan came about five minutes later, wearing a long gown that was neither gray nor white. He said, "You can rest assured and do the job. After it's done, I'll give you 10,000 yuan. This person is my enemy," and so on. After repeated interrogations, he insisted on his previous confession, which is consistent with the date of invitation and the room number of the Asia Hotel, as well as the circumstances of meeting the defendant and talking with him, as confessed by Zhao Guangfu in the police department on August 20th of this year. It can also be checked that when Zhao Guangfu reported Wang Xinggao to the police department on December 12th of last year, he also said that on June 16th, Zhou the Carpenter and Wang Xinggao led him to a room on the second floor of the Da Jiangnan Hotel, where he saw the defendant, who said that the assassination of Tang Jiapeng was instigated by the defendant. Although the Da Jiangnan Hotel was located in the Public Concession, which is different from the location he mentioned this time, according to Zhao Guangfu, Zhou the Carpenter said that the Asia Hotel was the Da Jiangnan Hotel. After this court sent police to investigate, it was reported that in the 19th year of the Republic [1930], the Asia Hotel was originally named the Jiangnan Hotel. Also, Zhou Shaolian, the waiter of the Asia Hotel, said that the Asia Hotel had more than 150 rooms, and Room 208 was on the second floor. Since the 21st year of the Republic [1932], the room numbers have not been changed. Therefore, Zhao Guangfu's statement that the previous confession of Da Jiangnan Hotel was the Asia Hotel is still credible. Moreover, Zhao Guangfu submitted a statement to this court on January 8th of this year, and in the murder file of Wang Xinggao and the draft of the self-accusation letter sent to the defendant, it was also written that Wang Xinggao was Wang Jinkui. On February 21st of this year, Zhao Guangfu's confession in this court also stated that "I said Wang Jinkui was Wang Xinggao when I was in custody." Although Zhang Tinggui had a teacher-student relationship with Wang Xinggao (Zhao Guangfu confessed in the police station on December 14th of last year that Zhang Tinggui was Wang Xinggao's disciple), he claimed in this court that he was invited by Wang Jinkui and insisted that he did not know Wang Xinggao, with the intention of protecting him. The circumstances are obvious. Zhao Guangfu also received money (Zhao Guangfu confessed on September 27th of this year that Wang Xinggao promised me money), and after the incident, he said that there were two people. However, judging from the above confessions, Wang Xinggao is Wang Jinkui, which is identifiable. Since Wang Xinggao and Wang Jinkui are the same person, it is even more proof that what Zhao Guangfu said about Wang Xinggao leading him to the Da Jiangnan Hotel was undoubtedly the Asia Hotel. Furthermore, Zhao Guangfu was questioned about why he did not mention what the defendant said when he was in the police station on December 14th of last year. He said, "What he said, I'm still waiting because the Supreme Court's official business hasn't come down yet." When asked why he previously confessed that the reward was 100 yuan, he replied, "I mentioned it in the British Concession. The confession had already been made, so I said what they said." It was found that the date of the Supreme Court's judgment on the case was December 29th of last year. Zhao Guangfu filed the case for investigation after Zhang Tinggui was arrested. Therefore, what he said is true. Looking at Zhao Guangfu's previous and subsequent statements, it is difficult to say that there are any doubts. Furthermore, Zhang Tinggui testified that on June 12th, 22nd year of the Republic [1933], he met Wang Jinkui on Chang'an Road in Zhabei. He said that he had something to ask me to help with. We talked about it in the teahouse. He said that it was the matter of Fourth Master Gu. From 10:00 PM to 11:00 PM on the 13th, Zhou Qifu led me to Room 208 of the Asia Hotel. When I went in, Fourth Master Gu was already in the room. He spoke to Wang Jinkui, but I didn't hear what he said. Later, Fourth Master Gu took out two pistols and handed them to Wang Jinkui. He said, "You can handle this matter. Wang Jinkui said, "He is the owner of the Tianchan Theater. The police station has already been taken care of. You can rest assured and do it. After it's done, I'll give you 10,000 yuan." Someone also said that Wang Jinkui said afterwards, "The higher-ups only sent down 400 yuan. You take some money first and hide in the countryside. I got 60 yuan." This is consistent with the situation described in the police department on September 2nd of this year. After repeated interrogations, Zhang Tinggui insisted on his previous words and refused to change his statement regarding the meeting with the defendant in the Asia Hotel and seeing the defendant hand over the pistol. Therefore, Zhang Tinggui's statement is also credible. The circumstances of the defendant instigating murder have been described in detail by Zhao Guangfu and Zhang Tinggui. Therefore, it is beyond doubt that Tang Jiapeng was killed by the defendant's instigation. Moreover, Zhao Guangfu repeatedly sent letters to the defendant in June and July of this year, demanding payment of the reward. After examining the letters (submitted by the defendants), they stated that "I have previously sent several letters, but have not received a reply. I was instructed by you to shoot Tang Jiapeng, and you personally promised a reward of 10,000 yuan. After the matter was completed perfectly, I was unable to contact you, and the reward could not be obtained. Unfortunately, I was arrested soon after and sentenced to life imprisonment. But I avenged you, exchanging my own life for money. Now that the revenge has been taken, not only is there no reward, but I am being ignored." Zhao Guangfu and the defendant did not know each other and had no grudges, as confessed by the defendant repeatedly. Also, the defendant claimed to be a legitimate businessman who occupied a prominent position in Shanghai society. If there was no instigation of murder, why would the prisoner Zhao Guangfu repeatedly demand a reward from the defendant? Moreover, according to Zhao Guangfu, while the case was on appeal, Xue Zhenyi was in the same detention center. He was the defendant's student and said that the defendant had hired lawyer Zhu to defend him, guaranteeing that he could be released from prison. After questioning Zhang Tinggui, he also confessed to the same situation. Although Xue Zhenyi argued that this was not the case, Xue Zhenyi's appeal for Zhang Tinggui has been admitted by him. Moreover, Xue Zhenyi sent a letter to Zheng Qian on April 2nd of this year, stating that "Zhao wants to falsely accuse the boss again, and he is proceeding in three steps." He also said, "My nephew, based on this, whether it happened before or not, regardless of whether it's related or not, has first explained to Zhao. Zhao said that he just wants the boss to provide assistance. If there is no relationship, you can ignore it. If there is a need for assistance, it is best to avoid it so that nothing else will happen." And in his letter to the defendant, he said, "I have used various words to explain to Zhao that since he was sentenced to life imprisonment, there is hope for him to be a human being in the future. Why should he make false accusations?" He said that he just wanted the adults to assist his family. My nephew promised Zhao to contact the Red Cross and ask friends to assist him, using this as an excuse, and he made it clear that he had to wait two weeks. If this matter is completely unrelated, you can ignore it. If it is slightly involved, it is better to avoid it beforehand to prevent the future. Moreover, Zhao was asked by the Westerner Qiao Huisi in the police station whether he knew someone like a certain adult. Zhao said he knew him. After my nephew questioned him, he really knew him. Now my nephew has copied Zhao's address. If you need to assist him, you can send someone to assist his family in the name of Zhao's old friend, so that nothing boring will happen." Another letter, sent on August 18th of this year, started with the words "Teacher Adult". It is clear that Xue Zhenyi and the defendant have a teacher-student relationship. It is very obvious that he is explaining things from the middle. All the above letters were submitted by the defendant as favorable evidence. Although Zhao Guangfu's letter ended with "If you are awakened or send a perennial consultant to come for a personal meeting, otherwise, I will first file a civil lawsuit to recover the reward, and then I will file a criminal lawsuit to defeat you. I really admire you," and also said, "I will make it so that you have difficulty defending yourself and difficulty expressing your grievances." However, this is a continuation of the previous text. The meaning of the words is nothing more than demanding a reward and being determined to get it. Using this as a reference, it is even more proof that the defendant has indeed committed the act of instigation. As for what Xue Zhenyi said, that he held a note from Zhao Guangfu asking him to testify, and that the prisoner Zhang Shuchuan was sufficient to prove the 3-7 split of the accounts, regardless of the fact that Zhao Guangfu firmly denied writing the note and that Zhao Guangfu repeatedly demanded rewards from the defendant and did not deny it, and that it was after he reported Wang Xinggao in December of last year, the defendant held this as evidence to refute Zhao Guangfu's blackmail and false accusation, which is obviously not credible. Moreover, Shanghai is a commercial center, and there are many people who own millions of assets. Why would Zhao Guangfu dare to accuse the defendant of a major murder case in order to achieve his purpose of defrauding money? If the defendant had nothing to do with it, why didn't he report his blackmail to the relevant authorities for investigation? According to the defendant, Zhang Tinggui is also unfamiliar and has no grudges. This can be asserted. After Zhang Tinggui was arrested and imprisoned, he did not demand any reward from the defendant. Therefore, it is obvious that he had no purpose of blackmail. Why would Zhang Tinggui give clear indications after repeated questioning? In summary, Zhao Guangfu and Zhang Tinggui's unfavorable statements against the defendant have been deemed to have no doubts and are credible. Then, the fact that the defendant instigated the murder of Tang Jiapeng is extremely clear, and there is no doubt that he should bear the criminal responsibility for murder. However, the new criminal law has been implemented and does not have a special provision for aggravated premeditated murder. Moreover, the defendant is already fifty years old, so he is sentenced to imprisonment at the court's discretion. The defendant in this case should be sentenced to fifteen years of imprisonment in accordance with Article 291 of the Criminal Procedure Law, Article 2, Paragraph 1, Article 29, Paragraph 1 and Paragraph 2, and Article 271, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law, and be deprived of civil rights for ten years in accordance with Article 37, Paragraph 2 of the Provisional Constitution. The judgment is specially made as the main text. The prosecutor of this case, Wang Ren, appeared in court and stated his opinions. If you do not agree with the judgment, you can file an appeal to the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court within ten days from the day after the judgment is served. (Omitted below) It is heard that the family of the defendant Gu Zhuxuan has hired a lawyer to write a statement to the Second Special Court, declaring an appeal, requesting that the case file be sent to the higher Third Branch of the High Court so that the reasons for the appeal can be corrected.

The elder brother has been arrested and sentenced in Tianjin, and the younger brother surrendered to the police in Shanghai.

An Wenping and An Wenpu, brothers from Beiping, were previously detained by the Shanghai Public Concession Police and sent to the First Special District Court for defrauding a large amount of antiques in Hong Kong, and were sentenced to a fine of 300 yuan. Bandits Send Letters, Scaring Jin Xinsan 112

Received four letters in succession, Lu Dehong admitted to writing them.

Jin Xinsan, the manager of the Chinese warehouse of the state-owned China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, lives at No. 8, Yongde Lane, Jielu. On August 31st of this year, Jin suddenly received an anonymous letter delivered by mail. Upon opening it, the words inside were threatening, attempting to extort 2,000 yuan. He was given a deadline of 6:00 PM to 8:00 PM on September 1st to negotiate at the intersection of Qiwupu Road and Kunming Road. If he did not agree, there would be danger to Jin's children in the future. Jin reported the letter to the Huishi Police Station, which sent detectives to wait, but no trace of the bandits was found. Subsequently, Jin received three more threatening letters in the past month, and the amount of money demanded gradually decreased. However, although the letters repeatedly arranged a place for negotiation, the bandits failed to appear, and the matter went on for more than a month without any progress in solving the case. It was not until 3:45 PM on the day before yesterday that the Chinese Detective Chief Shang Wu and Detective Wang Youshan of the Huishi Police Station arrested the suspects Lu Taotao and Zhang Er from Tongzhou on Kaifeng Road. Then, another accomplice, Lu Dehong, was arrested on Dixiwei Road and taken to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Eighth Criminal Court of the First Special Court. Police lawyer Zhang Tianyin, in addition to prosecuting them for attempted extortion in accordance with Article 346, Paragraph 3 of the Criminal Law, also stated the case, saying that the defendant Lu Dehong admitted in the police station that all four threatening letters were written by him alone. However, a certain Lu, who lives at No. 158, Sichuan Road, also received two threatening letters and reported them to the police station, but they have not yet been solved. However, the handwriting of the threatening letters received by the Lu mentioned above and those received by Jin Xinsan were found to be the same after examination by the Industrial Bureau's handwriting analysis department. Therefore, he requested that the case be postponed for continued investigation. Judge Wu Zehan briefly questioned the three defendants and ordered them to be remanded in custody, pending a postponement for further investigation.

The Chinese-Western Medicine Monthly is edited by the Chinese-Western Medicine Research Society. The society is a legitimate and complete medical research institution established this year. Therefore, the texts published are absolutely scientific and have no unqualified content. The printing paper is also meticulously made to achieve a high level of quality in both content and form. It was approved by the Central Ministry of Education the day before yesterday, and a notice was sent to all cultural institutions and schools in the country to purchase it. Its value is evident. The third issue of the magazine is published today. Chrysanthemum Competition at the New New Company Scheduled for Mid-Next Week 116

This year's flood was extremely severe, and the enthusiastic relief efforts from all walks of life followed one after another. Recently, the New New Company plans to take advantage of the initial blooming of chrysanthemums to hold a chrysanthemum competition to aid the disaster relief efforts. They drafted ten rules and sent them to the Yunnan Road Shanghai Disaster Relief Association to seek their approval. The rules are listed as follows: (1) Name: The New New Company's rooftop garden will hold a chrysanthemum competition to raise money for disaster relief. (2) Date: Choose any three days in the middle of next week. (3) Time: Every day from 9:00 AM to 12:00 PM. (4) Tickets: The price of each ticket is set at five jiao of silver. Your association will find a way to promote sales and send people to sell tickets at the entrance of our garden. All proceeds will be donated to disaster relief. (5) Chrysanthemums: In addition to our company's own hundreds of pots of various famous chrysanthemums being displayed free of charge, we plan to ask your association to invite various gardens to participate in the competition to expand the appeal. (6) Performances: Our company will hire famous performers to perform various wonderful performances to help out free of charge. All kinds of art displays will be provided by our company. (7) Flower sales: Whether the chrysanthemums are from our company or from the participating gardens, your association will send people to assist in selling them at the current market price. Half of the proceeds will be used for disaster relief. (8) Printing and publicity costs: In addition to our company's garden temporarily adapting the original New New Daily into a special issue for the chrysanthemum competition, which will be given away free of charge, the ticket fees and other advertising costs will be borne by your association. (9) The staff of our company's rooftop garden will voluntarily take on the duties of the organizers. Your association will send people to supervise and guide the various tasks. (10) Supplementary rules: If there are any imperfections, both parties will consult and negotiate at any time. It is heard that the Disaster Relief Association not only highly praised this initiative and replied with a letter requesting both parties to be jointly responsible for handling it, but also sent letters to famous gardens in Shanghai to participate in the competition and sent the association's Deputy Director Li Dachao to the site for supervision and guidance, with the assistance of three directors, Lu Deshen, Chen Wenkui, and Ge Yunsun. It is expected that there will be a lively atmosphere at that time, and people from all walks of life will be even more enthusiastic to participate for the sake of disaster relief and chrysanthemum appreciation, creating a grand occasion.

Minutes of the National Lixue Association Standing Committee Meeting 118

The China National Lixue (理教) Association held its 75th meeting yesterday, discussing the following: (1) A letter from the Jiangdu County Government of Jiangsu Province regarding the destruction of title deeds of the Yishantang (義善堂) public hall, along with grain tallies and land reports, requesting that they be forwarded for registration and filing. It was resolved to inform the public hall of this matter. (2) A letter from the Jing’antang (靜安堂) public hall of Zhoukou, Henan Province, reporting that it had been approved for filing by the Party and government authorities and submitting a list of elected officials for approval. It was resolved to approve it. (3) A letter from the Tianjin Lixue Association regarding the Deyi Tang (德一堂) public hall, which is a gathering place for heretical sects, requesting that it be denied membership. It was resolved to reply that it had already been decided that all public halls within the jurisdiction of Tianjin must join the association. (4) A letter from Yi Linsen (易霖森) and others from Xinghua, Jiangsu Province, stating that the Jishentang (集善堂) public hall had been ordered by the county Party headquarters to organize a branch, but the initiators were of complex backgrounds, and the four leading figures were all smokers and drinkers, publicly posting announcements all over the streets, thus disgracing the reputation of Lixue, requesting instructions. It was resolved to reply that the association is of a united nature and does not have branch names, so the blame does not lie with the association. (5) A letter from Wang Desheng (王德聲), director of the Yishantang (一善堂) public hall in Dong'an, Hebei Province, stating that he has been studying Lixue for thirty-eight years, enclosing a copy of the Five-Character Method up to the Fifty-Three-Character Leading the Masses Great Method, requesting verification. It was resolved to discuss it at length at the next meeting. (6) A letter from the Songbaitang (松柏堂) public hall in Nanchang, Jiangxi Province, reporting that the leaders of the masses were being humiliated and requesting assistance. It was resolved to write an official letter to the Nanchang Municipal Public Security Bureau. (7) A letter from the Jinghetang (靜和堂) public hall in Qinghe, Hebei Province, requesting that a notice be issued to safeguard them. It was resolved to pass it. (8) A letter from the Shanghai Lixue Association regarding the matter of Wang Huiyou (王會友), a member of the Zixing Tang (自醒堂) public hall, being innocently implicated, requesting assistance. It was resolved to write to the Supreme Court for verification. (9) A letter from the Zixiutang (自修堂) public hall in Nanzhang, Hubei Province, requesting that the authorities be asked to provide protection. It was resolved to write an official letter to the Nanzhang County Government. (The rest omitted.)

The 254th inspection was held at the Issuing Bureau of this bank on October 26, 1935. The inspection results are reported as follows: (A) The total amount of exchange certificates issued was 131,246,364 silver dollars, including 120,607,994 silver dollar certificates and 10,638,370 subsidiary currency certificates. The total amount of exchange certificate reserve was 131,246,364 silver dollars, including 101,857,964 silver dollars in cash reserve. This cash reserve included 90,700,841.18 yuan stored in the issuing vault of this bank, 101 yuan stored in the issuing branch, 2,211,367 yuan stored in various branches, 7,918,179 yuan stored with fellow banks, and 29,388,400 silver dollars in guarantee reserve. (B) The total amount of customs gold unit exchange certificates issued was 373,324.7 yuan. The total amount of customs gold unit exchange certificate reserve was 373,324.7 yuan. This reserve included 7,351.95 taels of standard gold, equivalent to 373,324.7 yuan in customs gold units at a fixed price of 5.0779. According to Article 22 of the Central Bank Law, the cash reserve should be at least 60%, and the remainder should be guaranteed by legal guarantee products. The inspection results showed that the cash reserve exceeded 60%, and the guarantee reserve was within 40%, which is in compliance with the law. This report is hereby made. October 28, 1935, Chairman of the Board of Supervisors of the Central Bank Li Fuxun, Supervisors Xie Mengjun, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Jiqing.

Commercial News

Finance: Public Panic; Gold Market "Government Bonds" 125

Assassination News Causes Selling Pressure, Prices Fall to 0.06 Yuan. Exchange Rates Unmoved, Easily Raised, Still Increase by 10 Yuan

Yesterday, the gold market remained uneasy, actions were abnormal, and trends moved towards "government bonds". Initially, news of the assassination of Wang Jingwei and Zhang Jingyao in Nanjing stirred up selling pressure. Many parties unloaded, prices plummeted. The public panicked because buyers had been relying on the Sixth Plenary Session as a chance for rumors to thrive. It became fatigued and prices fell to 1106 yuan. Unfortunately, the exchange rates remained unchanged and were easily pulled up, resulting in a rebound higher than the previous day. This morning, overseas silver markets in England and the United States were stable. Silver prices in Montreux were barely up or down, as were exchange rates. Gold prices in London rose by one penny. Public sentiment was still good because speculators had driven up prices in overnight trading to over 80 yuan. Although pre-market trading opened at 80 yuan, there was no sustaining. Heng Yu Fu (恒餘福) and Yong (永) sold to 70 yuan. Heng Yu Han (恒餘涵), Heng Yu Qing (恒餘慶), Yong Fu Xing (永福興), and Yong Heng Xing (永恒興) bought low. Prices rose to 78 yuan. Fu Xing (福興), Yong Da (永大), De Cheng (德成) continued to sell, then prices dropped to 73-74 yuan. The Central Bank announced its official exchange rates, which decreased for both British and American currencies. Customs Gold Units rose by 3.5 cents. The standard gold price was posted at 1093.4 yuan. After opening, the market was stable and prices broke through the 80 yuan level. Chinese merchants were selling. It was anticipated that HSBC would post higher rates, with British currency up by 1.25 and American currency up by 0.25. Prices gradually decreased. However, because banks were still buying, there were multiple transactions in the middle, and exchange rates hardened. Unfavorable rumors circulated, and prices eventually fell below 60 yuan. Banks continued to buy, and buyers were still active, so prices gradually rebounded by nearly 20 yuan. However, because of the sluggish Hong Kong market, prices soon gradually decreased again from above 70 yuan. When Reuters reported that the assassination of Wang Jingwei and Zhang Jingyao had no special impact, public sentiment became abnormal and followed the trend, with many parties rushing to unload. Selling pressure was strong. It was predicted that Indian silver would rise by 3 annas, but prices fell to 1106 yuan. Speculators covered their short positions at low prices. At noon, prices rose to above 30 yuan. The afternoon market was firm due to the raising of prices by Fu Xing Yong (福興永) and Da De Cheng (大德成). After the opening, buyers were eager and prices continued to rise. However, due to HSBC's unloading, prices once fell back to below 40 yuan. Banks had a flat appetite, but public sentiment was still good, so prices were held. Indian silver decreased by 3 annas and broke through the 60 yuan level. Although there were many pullbacks after that, because the Hong Kong market softened and Indian silver decreased by another small 2 annas, prices finally rose again to above 70 yuan. Securities: News from the Capital Causes Public Bonds to Crash 129

Only Two Trading Sessions Done All Day, Market Extremely Chaotic. Private Trading Fluctuates Two to Three Yuan Above and Below the Limit-Down Price. Troop Reduction and Long-Term Rehabilitation Uniquely Trending Upward.

Yesterday, the Chinese Securities Exchange experienced a major market upheaval. At times, it was like a raging storm, with prices plummeting to the limit-down. At other times, it was calm and clear, with vigorous buying activity and fear of being left behind. Only two trading sessions were held throughout the day, and the difference between the high and low prices was like heaven and earth. This kind of market was unprecedented. The sudden arrival of news of the assassination in the capital cast a dark shadow over the market. Short sellers emerged, displaying unusual bravery, as if a major disaster was about to occur. Long positions, however, had not lost hope and continued to push prices up. Therefore, the future situation was impossible to predict. Although the environment was harsh, the long positions seemed unconcerned. If they were to unload their positions, the danger would be difficult to estimate.

Yesterday's trading started late, after 11:00 am, due to the excessive number of accounts from the previous night. The severity of the situation was an unprecedented change in the past twenty-four years.

Yarn and Cotton 131

Yarn Prices Fall and Then Recover 132

Initially, the Assassination Telegram Caused a Sharp Decline, Followed by a Rise Due to Increased Tender Prices

The yarn market experienced sharp declines and advances, and the situation remained turbulent. Market sentiment was chaotic and inconsistent. Initially, news of President Wang's assassination in Nanjing caused market tremors and a surge in selling pressure, leading to an immediate sharp decline in prices. In the afternoon, the market turned higher, with the pace quickening due to large purchases by a certain bank under a code name. Rumors of rising tender prices and currency inflation intensified, and the market rebounded. However, actual demand remained sluggish.

Tender Prices Fell in the Morning and Recovered in the Afternoon

At the opening of the yarn market, prices for all months fell consistently due to a noticeable reversal in the rising trend of tender prices. Market sentiment weakened, and the number of buyers on the floor decreased, with some long positions closing out and prices falling. However, securities firms engaged in aggressive buying, purchasing large amounts, which helped maintain market prices. Prices recovered by several cents in the second session. In the third session, rumors suddenly emerged, and news of the assassination spread, causing a major shock to the market. Selling pressure intensified, and prices plummeted. As a result, prices for all months fell by 3.6 to 5.1 yuan compared to the previous day's closing prices.

The market suddenly reversed and turned higher at the opening of the afternoon session. The situation became tense, with reports that tender prices had fallen to a low of 1107 yuan in the morning and then jumped back to over 1150 yuan in the afternoon. Rumors of currency inflation became more prevalent, and the code-named bank resumed buying activities. The market became short of supply, and prices continued to rise. As a result, prices for all months rose by 2.7 to 3.9 yuan compared to the morning's closing prices.

The sold brands were Mingde (1450 bales), He Xing (1450 bales), Shen Ji (1550 bales), Ren Feng (2000 bales), Run Kang (2450 bales), Da Ji (850 bales), and Yu Da (1100 bales). The purchased brands were Yu Da (1400 bales), Jin Chang (6950 bales), Geng Feng (1100 bales), Shen Chang (1250 bales), Da Chang Cheng (1300 bales), Tong He (1150 bales), Da Fu (2150 bales), and Chang Feng (1500 bales). The cotton market experienced a sharp decline in the morning and a recovery in the afternoon, with prices fluctuating up and down. The market situation was extremely chaotic. Initially, there were signs of a reversal in the rising gold prices, and rumors about the political situation were rampant, leading to a sharp decline in prices. In the afternoon, the code-named bank resumed aggressive buying, and the buying pressure was particularly strong, causing the market to rebound.

The Code-Named Bank Purchased Cotton

At the opening of the cotton market, prices for all months trended downward consistently. This was mainly due to concerns about a potential reversal after days of sharp increases, and the decline in tender prices also dampened market sentiment. There were more sellers, and prices trended downward. By the close of the morning session, selling pressure intensified due to reports of a serious assassination attempt on a prominent figure, and tender prices plummeted to 1107 yuan. A sudden surge of sellers appeared, and the downward momentum was sharp. As a result, prices for near-term contracts fell by 90 cents, and prices for far-term contracts fell by 2.2 yuan.

The market experienced a rapid change at the opening of the afternoon session, and buying interest suddenly became strong. A certain bank made large purchases, and the code-named bank continued to aggressively buy, purchasing 15,500 bales. Prices rose gradually, and it was said that rising tender prices were favorable to long positions, and the rumors were booming, further strengthening the buying pressure. As a result, prices for all months rose by 50 cents to 2.5 yuan compared to the morning's closing prices.

Little Change in Yarn and Cotton Grades for April 1936 133

The Shanghai Yarn and Cloth Exchange held its 125th Cotton Yarn Grading Meeting on October 28th to grade yarn for delivery in April 1936. The results of the review showed no changes in the grades of the 20s yarn, which remained the same as the grades for March. However, the grades of the 16s and 10s Double Fish yarn produced by Wuxi Qingfeng were raised by one yuan. The previous discount of 16 yuan was changed to 15 yuan, and the 10s Double Fish yarn was also raised by one yuan, with the previous discount of 41 yuan changed to 40 yuan. The grades of substitute cotton used for delivery in April 1936 were the same as the grades for March, with no changes.

Overseas Cotton Market Mostly Down, Few Up 134

Yesterday, trading on the US cotton market was light, with most activity focused on switching contracts. Initially, there was hesitation among traders due to hedging activity. However, reports of potential frost damage in the western and northern regions of the cotton belt caused a slight rebound, with some foreign firms making purchases. Traders needed January contracts, and prices then stabilized as manufacturers and speculators entered the market with limit orders. Spot prices rose by 5 points, and futures prices rose by 2 to 7 points. Only the October contract fell by 5 points.

English cotton spot prices fell by 8 points, and futures prices fell by 1 to 3 points. The Indian cotton market was overturned by Japanese firms selling and speculators buying. Prices then weakened due to long covering. As a result, Pingguore fell by 1.75 rupees, Omla fell by 1 to 1.5 rupees, and White Luo Creek fell by 1.75 rupees.

Grains: Flour and Wheat Plunge Together, Grain Exchange Suspends Trading Before Noon Due to Margin Calls 135

Auction of Foreign-Owned Sesame Seeds Today

There was a huge change in flour market opening prices this morning. Initially, foreign wheat prices rebounded by 30 cents, and the market consensus was still bullish. It was naturally easy for the market to become agitated. As a result, the opening price for this month was as high as 96 cents. However, seeing this high price, the market immediately turned downward. The opening price fell to 92.5 cents. Although the opening price for long-term contracts was good, with an increase of only 2-3 cents compared to the end of the previous month, by the third session, due to the news of President Wang's assassination and the sharp fall in the gold market, market sentiment was in chaos, and prices for all months plunged. By the close of trading, prices for all months had fallen by about 10 cents compared to the opening. Approximately one million bags were traded in half a day.

When trading resumed in the afternoon, prices recovered by 5-6 cents due to short covering and continued buying by outside long positions. The opening price for March was 3.0775 yuan, but the closing price also fell to 3.01 yuan. Going forward, the political situation may cause further turmoil.

Domestic and Foreign Rice Prices Rise Together 136

(Shanghai South) Yesterday, more than twenty domestic rice boats arrived. Market conditions, buoyed by rising confidence, led to a sharp increase in prices. Retail activity was very active. Indica rice prices rose by 30-40 cents, and new japonica rice prices rose by 40-50 cents. Merchants purchased a total of 400-500 bags.

(Shanghai North) Yesterday, the northern rice market was affected by soaring flour prices and active purchases, while the four villages were busy with agricultural work, resulting in weak shipments. Only about 30 boats arrived at the river docks. Shop inventories were low, and morning trading was very good, with prices increasing by 30-40 cents. Although shop sentiment weakened later, the river docks' inventories were gradually depleted, leading to a sharp increase of 40-60 cents for new japonica rice. Yangbu tip rice also rose by 40-50 cents, Dujian rice rose by 20-30 cents, Yaocong tip rice rose by 30-40 cents, and Baiyuan rice also rose by 10-20 cents. Prices of other rice varieties followed suit, rising by 20-30 cents.

Yesterday, there was strong interest in the Indica rice market. Morning trading was still active. However, after the news of President Wang's assassination was published in the newspapers, buyers mostly waited and watched. As a result, transactions were not as active as in previous days. However, demand from Tianjin was still strong. A total of 1572 bags of Ningbo, Ji, Wan, and Liu Indica rice were sold on the market, along with dozens of bags of Taizhou rice. Ningbo and Hubei white rice were also purchased by local retailers. Therefore, Ningbo rice continued to rise by 20 cents. As merchants waited and watched in the afternoon, the market turned flat. A total of 1300 bags of Jiangxi rice, 2000 bags of Ningbo rice, 73 bags of Taizhou rice, 976 bags of Hankou rice, 1000 bags of Guangdong rice, and 250 bags of Hangzhou rice were sold throughout the day. With the exception of shipments to Tianjin, only 300-400 bags were sold to retailers, while the rest were purchased by merchants.

Foreign rice stocks were low, and old inventories were being held back. New inventories were highly sought after, and market transactions were increasingly quiet. Yesterday, 300 bags of old Wulong rice and 200 bags of Siamese Yuan rice were repurchased by local merchants. Prices also rose by about 10 cents.

Sports News

World Tennis Star Ko Hin Performs in Canton 137

Combining Intelligence and Skill to Reach Perfection, Chinese and Western Audiences Alike Exclaim in Awe

(Special Dispatch from Guangzhou) World-renowned professional tennis player Ko Hin recently toured the East. He arrived in the Philippines at the end of last month and began competing against the top Filipino tennis players on the second of this month. Mr. Ko won all seven matches, completely subduing the Filipino tennis champions. The entire Philippines was filled with admiration. After the competitions in the Philippines, Mr. Ko, despite having defeated the Philippine tennis champion Aragan, greatly admired Aragan's skill. He invited Aragan, along with the Filipino tennis talent Gavias, to travel to Sydney, Australia. At the same time, he invited Shanghai's professional tennis player Cavanaugh to meet in Hong Kong to prepare for departure. Mr. Ko and his party of three arrived in Hong Kong on the 25th aboard the President McKinley. In response to an invitation from the Guangzhou Municipal Sports Association, they will hold exhibition matches and visit the construction projects in Guangdong Province. After resting in Hong Kong for a day, they took a Hong Kong steamer to Guangzhou on the evening of the 26th, arriving in Guangzhou on the morning of the 27th. In the morning, they toured the famous sites of Guangzhou and visited various construction projects. Afterwards, they attended a welcome reception hosted by the Municipal Sports Association. Consuls from various countries stationed in Guangdong, as well as overseas Chinese from countries such as France, England, and Germany, enthusiastically attended the event, making it an unprecedented grand gathering in international social events. This was because people from various countries had long admired Mr. Ko's reputation and considered it fortunate to witness Mr. Ko's brilliance and appreciate his tennis skills.

An Unprecedented Spectacle The competition took place at the tennis court of the Municipal Sports Association in Central Park at 3 p.m. this afternoon. Three matches were scheduled, with the first and second matches being singles, and the third match being doubles. Tickets were divided into three categories: one yuan, two yuan, and three yuan. After noon, ticket buyers entered the venue in an endless stream. In front of the Sports Association, carriages and horses were bustling, and Chinese and Western ladies were shoulder to shoulder, extremely crowded. Before 3 p.m., tickets were already sold out. Those who arrived later stood behind the seats, and those who watched from afar outside the venue were no less than a thousand people.

Mr. Ko Takes the Stage At precisely 3 p.m., the referees took the stage. First, Aragan (Philippines) and Cavanaugh (Shanghai) competed in a singles match. Aragan was energetic, experienced, and had superior skills, defeating Cavanaugh with a score of six to one. The first match was still a singles match. French Ko Hin appeared amidst the applause and cheers of the audience. Reporters from various countries rushed forward to take photos of Mr. Ko. He had a prominent nose and deep-set eyes, possessing a calm mind, and at first glance, he was known as a famous general with both intelligence and skill. His opponent was the German, Bin Diga, an overseas Chinese in Guangdong (a rising star in Guangzhou's tennis world).

World Professional Tennis Player Ko Hin Performs in Guangzhou (Left: Mr. Ko; Right: German Bao Diga)

Supernatural Skill After the start of the match, Ko Hin performed brilliantly, repeatedly trapping Bao Diga. His blocking, drawing, and pressing of the ball all had unique advantages. Sometimes, he used light wrists to send the ball over the net, leaving the opponent unable to reach it in time. Sometimes, he used lightning-fast strokes, the ball was fast and powerful, making the opponent unable to defend. His one-handed operation was unpredictable. In tense moments, the opponent ran all over the court, struggling to parry, while Mr. Ko faced it calmly, standing like Mount Tai, moving like a startled rabbit. Even if the opponent had dangerous and urgent balls, he could still handle them with ease. Mr. Ko was not only known for his ball skills, but also often spotted the opponent's weaknesses, taking advantage of flaws and gaps, using the ball magically. He truly had both "skill" and "intelligence." His opponent Bao Diga was not weak either, but when he met Mr. Ko, it was like a small witch seeing a great witch. In half an hour of hard fighting, he lost to Ko Hin with a score of six to three.

Doubles Performance The third match was a doubles exhibition match. Aragan (Philippines) and Gavias (Philippines) formed a team, while Ko Hin cooperated with Bao Diga. They played a total of three sets. In the first set, Ko Hin served, winning every point, with a score of six to two. In the second set, Aragan was young and brave, shaking his spirits and adopting an offensive, winning back a set with a score of six to three. In the third set, Ko's team gradually weakened. After Bao Diga fought hard against Ko Hin in the previous match, he was already exhausted. Cooperating with Ko Hin again, his strength was even more unsustainable. On the contrary, Aragan took advantage of his remaining courage, launching wave after wave of attacks. At this time, Ko Hin repeatedly used his volleying skills to pull back a few points, but he could not support it alone. Aragan's team then won the third set with a score of six to three. In the doubles summary, Aragan's team finally won.

Leaving Canton for Hong Kong It was already 6 p.m. in the afternoon, and dusk was approaching. The audience then cheered and dispersed. In the evening, the Municipal Sports Association hosted a banquet for Ko Hin and the Philippine athletes. Ko and others left Canton for Hong Kong on the 28th. From the 28th to the 30th, there will be exhibition matches at the Kowloon Ball Club in Hong Kong every afternoon at 3 p.m. At the beginning of next month, they will take a British postal ship to Australia. (Evening of October 27)

Municipal No. 1 Stadium - Registration Period for the Industrial and Commercial Football Club 144

Begins Tomorrow, Deadline on the 20th

The Municipal No. 1 Public Stadium's 7th Industrial and Commercial Amateur Football Competition has now finalized its regulations. Registration for old members will begin on the 3rd of this month and end on the 20th. After the registration deadline, if there are any remaining slots, they will be supplemented by new member registrations. Due to the limited venue, it is feared that there will be no way to manage if there are too many teams. There are also the following restrictions on the registration of old members: (1) The qualifications of old members are limited to the football teams that participated in the last (6th) competition; (2) Teams that participated in the last competition and have fewer than ten old players will not be considered old members; (3) Teams that participated in the last competition and forfeited twice will not be entitled to registration; (4) Teams or players who participated in the last competition and insulted the referee, showed animosity towards the opposing team, or committed fraudulent acts will not be entitled to registration; (5) Players who participated in the last competition and are enrolled in school or are employed as physical education teachers will not be entitled to registration; (6) The registration of each team's players is limited to sixteen people. If the number of old players is insufficient, new players may be added to supplement the team, but the number of supplemented players may not exceed six people. Supplemented players must be non-students and not employed as physical education professionals. As for the registration procedures, registration forms can be obtained from the association, filled out in detail, and accompanied by a six-inch photo of all players. If there are any omissions, individual photos should be added. It is also heard that this year's competition will be quite strict. Any barbaric behavior, intentional harm to opponents, and refusal to obey the referee's decisions will result in the disqualification of the entire team from the competition.

Ministry of Education Actively Improving Medical Education 147

Establishing a Special Committee to Unify Authority

In addition to frequently sending commissioners and inspectors and occasionally sending section chiefs to various provinces and cities to conduct on-site inspections and guidance, the Ministry of Education's inspection of medical education in the past was always based on temporary requests to experts for inspection (such as Pang Jingzhou, etc.). Unlike sending a ministerial commissioner, the inspection time and duration were inevitably somewhat difficult (temporary requests were based on courtesy, and the individuals requested all had other work and could not therefore neglect their original careers for long. If the Ministry of Education encountered urgent inspection matters, it had no staff members and it was more inconvenient to ask people). Furthermore, those who handled medical education in the Ministry on a regular basis were all doing it on a part-time basis, with no specific responsibility. Therefore, in addition to establishing two specialized committees for midwifery education and nursing education under the original Ministry of Education Medical Education Committee based on the resolutions of the Medical Education Committee, the Ministry of Education also changed the Elementary and Secondary School Health Education Design Committee to be under the Medical Education Committee, unifying authority in order to connect and communicate and facilitate progress. Normally, the Ministry of Education has several committees for medical education, and Zhu Zhanggeng and Nie Yuchan, etc., regularly work in the ministry, so their responsibilities are more specific and things are easier to accomplish. The Ministry of Education had previously sent personnel to inspect hospitals, midwifery schools, nursing schools and colleges, and an assistant training class in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Shanghai provinces and cities. Now, it is continuing to send personnel to inspect other provinces and cities. Now we see the Department of Orders assigning Yang Chongrui to inspect the midwifery school in Guangdong Province, and the Department of Orders has instructed the Guangdong Provincial Department of Education to inform them.

The presiding group included Tong Xingbai, Du Gang, and Leng Xueqiao, with Luo Lie as the master of ceremonies. Performing the rituals as scheduled, first, all the Boy Scouts recited the oath, followed by a report by the chairman, speeches by Tong Wei, the representative of the Municipal Party Department, and Du Gang, the representative of Director Pan of the Municipal Education Bureau. Then, they shouted "Long Live" three times and dispersed after singing the Boy Scout song.

Jinling Women's University 20th Anniversary 149

Jinling Women's University in Nanjing was founded in 1915. In 1930, it was renamed Jinling Women's College of Arts and Sciences, the only women's higher education institution in central China. Since its founding, it has been 20 years. A grand commemorative ceremony was held today. At the same time, because Mrs. De Benkang, the founder of the school, is celebrating her 60th birthday, the graduates of the school returned to the school one after another to celebrate Mrs. De's birthday at noon today. At 3:30 p.m., a 20th anniversary celebration was held. In addition to the administrative chief's training speech, President Sun Zhesheng of the Legislative Yuan and President Luo Jialun of the Central University were invited to speak. Furthermore, the school authorities, believing that most of the graduating students are working in various middle schools, and this gathering is a rare opportunity, held a secondary education discussion meeting for the benefit of the students, and invited the principals of various middle schools in Nanjing to participate. The time was from 9 a.m. to 12 p.m. today, and Mr. Liao Maoru, Ai Xizhou, and others were invited to speak. Tomorrow morning, President Zhang Boling of Nankai University will be invited to speak. In the afternoon, the annual meeting of the alumni association will be held. The day after tomorrow morning, the graduating students will visit the new construction of the capital. In the afternoon, the secondary education discussion meeting will continue, and there will be a celebration entertainment party in the evening, which can be called a grand event.
